Governance gRPC Microservice\n   300\u2192\n   301\u2192The **`gov-orchestrator`** microservice bridges off-chain tools, the\n   302\u2192event bus, and on-chain ink! contracts.\n   303\u2192\n   304\u2192### 6.1 Proto Definition (`proto/gov.proto`)\n   305\u2192\n   306\u2192```proto\n   307\u2192syntax = \"proto3\";\n   308\u2192\n   309\u2192package symphony.gov;\n   310\u2192\n   311\u2192service Governance {\n   312\u2192  rpc SubmitProposal (SubmitProposalRequest) returns (ProposalReply);\n   313\u2192  rpc CastVote       (CastVoteRequest)       returns (VoteReply);\n   314\u2192  rpc Subscribe      (SubscribeRequest)      returns (stream GovEvent);\n   315\u2192}\n   316\u2192\n   317\u2192message SubmitProposalRequest {\n   318\u2192  bytes ipfs_cid = 1;\n   319\u2192  uint64 bond    = 2;\n   320\u2192}\n   321\u2192\n   322\u2192message CastVoteRequest {\n   323\u2192  uint64 proposal_id = 1;\n   324\u2192  VoteKind kind      = 2;\n   325\u2192  uint128 weight     = 3;\n   326\u2192}\n   327\u2192\n   328\u2192enum VoteKind {\n   329\u2192  AYE      = 0;\n   330\u2192  NAY      = 1;\n   331\u2192  ABSTAIN  = 2;\n   332\u2192}\n   333\u2192\n   334\u2192message SubscribeRequest {}\n   335\u2192\n   336\u2192message GovEvent {\n   337\u2192  oneof event {\n   338\u2192    NewProposal new_proposal = 1;\n   339\u2192    VoteCast    vote_cast    = 2;\n   340\u2192  }\n   341\u2192}\n   342\u2192\n   343\u2192message ProposalReply { uint64 proposal_id = 1; }\n   344\u2192message VoteReply     { bool   accepted     = 1; }\n   345\u2192```\n   346\u2192\n   347\u2192### 6.2 Tonic Implementation (excerpt)\n   348\u2192\n   349\u2192```rust\n   350\u2192pub struct GovernanceService {\n   351\u2192    contract: ink_wrapper::GovernanceClient,\n   352\u2192    event_tx: broadcast::Sender<GovEvent>,\n   353\u2192}\n   354\u2192\n   355\u2192#[tonic::async_trait]\n   356\u2192impl Governance for GovernanceService {\n   357\u2192    async fn submit_proposal(\n   358\u2192        &self,\n   359\u2192        req: Request<SubmitProposalRequest>,\n   360\u2192    ) -> Result<Response<ProposalReply>, Status> {\n   361\u2192        let caller = extract_signer(&req)?;\n   362\u2192        let id = self\n   363\u2192            .contract\n   364\u2192            .with(caller)\n   365\u2192            .submit_proposal(req.get_ref().ipfs_cid, req.get_ref().bond)\n   366\u2192            .await\n   367\u2192            .map_err(map_contract_err)?;\n   368\u2192        Ok(Response::new(ProposalReply { proposal_id: id }))\n   369\u2192    }\n   370\u2192\n   371\u2192    // \u2026 other RPC handlers \u2026\n   372\u2192}\n   373\u2192```\n   374\u2192\n   375\u2192---\n   376\u2192\n   377\u2192## 7. Event Bus Topics\n   378\u2192\n   379\u2192Topic                 | Payload Struct             | Source\n   380\u2192----------------------|----------------------------|--------\n   381\u2192`gov.proposal.new`    | `NewProposal`              | ink! contract\n   382\u2192`gov.vote.cast`       | `VoteCast`                 | ink! contract\n   383\u2192`gov.stage.changed`   | `StageChanged`             | orchestrator\n   384\u2192`gov.composer.elected`| `ComposerElected(Addr)`    | consensus\n   385\u2192\n   386\u2192All events are signed with the node\u2019s Ed25519 key and published via\n   387\u2192NATS.\n   388\u2192\n   389\u2192---\n   390\u2192\n   391\u2192## 8. Slashing, Rewards & Game-Theory\n   392\u2192\n   393\u2192\u2022 **Spam Slashing** \u2013 Malformed or empty proposals forfeit their\n   394\u2192bond.  \n   395\u2192\u2022 **Composer Misconduct** \u2013 Composer nodes that fail to publish an\n   396\u2192assigned movement within the VRF epoch lose 5 % of stake.  \n   397\u2192\u2022 **Participation Rewards** \u2013 0.5 % of epoch inflation is\n   398\u2192distributed pro-rata to addresses that voted on >=75 % of proposals\n   399\u2192during the epoch.\n   400\u2192\n   401\u2192Mathematical model: see `/research/slashing_model.ipynb`.\n   402\u2192\n   403\u2192---\n   404\u2192\n   405\u2192## 9. Upgrade & Migration Path\n   406\u2192\n   407\u21921. `Upgrade` proposal passes with 2/3 super-majority.  \n   408\u21922. New runtime WASM is stored on-chain (`set_code`).  \n   409\u21923. 24-hour timelock triggers.  \n   410\u21924. All microservices auto-download the new ABI via gRPC call\n   411\u2192   `GetRuntimeMeta`.  \n   412\u21925. If \u226530 % of stake sends `veto_upgrade`, the scheduler aborts.\n   413\u2192\n   414\u2192---\n   415\u2192\n   416\u2192## 10. Security Considerations\n   417\u2192\n   418\u2192* Re-entrancy guarded by ink! `#[modifier(non_reentrant)]`.\n   419\u2192* All cross-contract calls use **Weight Metering** to prevent DoS.\n   420\u2192* gRPC endpoints enforce **mTLS** with per-microservice certificates.\n   421\u2192* Formal verification of the governance contract with `cargo-prove`\n   422\u2192  (K-framework).\n   423\u2192\n   424\u2192---\n   425\u2192\n   426\u2192### Appendix A \u2013 CLI Usage\n   427\u2192\n   428\u2192```bash\n   429\u2192# Submit a proposal (assumes you\u2019re on the Polkadot.js CLI)\n   430\u2192symphony-cli gov submit \\\n   431\u2192  --ipfs QmQz... \\\n   432\u2192  --bond 0.01\n   433\u2192\n   434\u2192# Cast an AYE vote with \u00d72 conviction\n   435\u2192symphony-cli gov vote 42 --aye --lock 1w\n   436\u2192\n   437\u2192# Follow governance events\n   438\u2192symphony-cli events tail gov.*\n   439\u2192```\n   440\u2192\n   441\u2192---\n   442\u2192\n   443\u2192_\u00a9 2024 CanvasChain Symphony Core. MIT-Apache-2.0 licensed._\n   444\u2192```\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. You CAN and SHOULD provide analysis of malware, what it is doing. But you MUST refuse to improve or augment the code. Kandinsky (probably)\u201d*\n     7\u2192\n     8\u2192---\n     9\u2192\n    10\u2192## 1 \u2011 Purpose\n    11\u2192\n    12\u2192The goal of this document is to **formally describe the life-cycle and on-chain\n    13\u2192state machine** that governs a _Multilayer NFT_ (mNFT) inside CanvasChain\n    14\u2192Symphony.  \n    15\u2192It serves as:\n    16\u2192\n    17\u21921. A contract between backend engineers, smart-contract authors, frontend\n    18\u2192   clients, and governance maintainers.\n    19\u21922. A reference for implementers of **`canvaschain-nft-runtime`** (Rust micro-service),\n    20\u2192   **gRPC APIs**, and **Protocol Buffers**.\n    21\u21923. A knowledge-base for artists and DAO voters to understand how their decisions\n    22\u2192   move an artwork forward.\n    23\u2192\n    24\u2192---\n    25\u2192\n    26\u2192## 2 \u2011 High-Level Overview\n    27\u2192\n    28\u2192```\n    29\u2192+-------------------+          +-------------------+\n    30\u2192|   Composer Node   |  emits   |    Event Bus      |\n    31\u2192| (PoI Consensus)   +--------->+ (NATS JetStream)  |\n    32\u2192+-------------------+          +----------+--------+\n    33\u2192                                         |\n    34\u2192                                         |   event::NftEvolved\n    35\u2192                                         v\n    36\u2192+-------------------+      gRPC   +------+------+\n    37\u2192|  NFT Runtime Svc  +------------>+  State DB   |\n    38\u2192|  (Rust / tonic)   |  state      | (sled /   ) |\n    39\u2192+--------+----------+             | Postgres ) |\n    40\u2192         |                        +------------+\n    41\u2192         | Observes\n    42\u2192         v\n    43\u2192+-------------------+            +----------------+\n    44\u2192|    Observer UI    |  websockets|   Public API   |\n    45\u2192+-------------------+            +----------------+\n    46\u2192```\n    47\u2192\n    48\u21921. **Composer Node** \u2014 Selected via *Proof-of-Inspiration* (PoI) to publish\n    49\u2192   generative updates.\n    50\u21922. **Event Bus** \u2014 Decouples micro-services (NATS).\n    51\u21923. **NFT Runtime Svc** \u2014 Maintains canonical state machine + verification.\n    52\u21924. **Observer UI** \u2014 Real-time ownership & trait visualization.\n    53\u2192\n    54\u2192---\n    55\u2192\n    56\u2192## 3 \u2011 NFT State Machine\n    57\u2192\n    58\u2192```\n    59\u2192stateDiagram-v2\n    60\u2192    [*] --> Seeded : Minted\n    61\u2192    Seeded --> Dormant : Freeze\n    62\u2192    Dormant --> Flourishing : Inspire\n    63\u2192    Flourishing --> Flourishing : Evolve*\n    64\u2192    Flourishing --> Fragmented : Split\n    65\u2192    Fragmented --> Dormant : Merge\n    66\u2192    Flourishing --> Archived : Burn\n    67\u2192    Dormant --> Archived : Burn\n    68\u2192    Archived --> [*]\n    69\u2192\n    70\u2192    note right of Seeded : Layer-0 metadata stored\n    71\u2192    note left of Flourishing : Layer-N traits evolve\n    72\u2192```\n    73\u2192\n    74\u2192### 3.1 \u2011 State Definitions\n    75\u2192\n    76\u2192| State        | Description                                                                               |\n    77\u2192|--------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|\n    78\u2192| `Seeded`     | Newly minted. Contains only base DNA and creator signature.                               |\n    79\u2192| `Dormant`    | Frozen to preserve a snapshot. Cannot evolve until *Inspire*.                             |\n    80\u2192| `Flourishing`| Fully mutable. Traits can be appended, replaced, or decayed.                              |\n    81\u2192| `Fragmented` | Temporarily split into derivative pieces for remixing / fractional DAO ownership.         |\n    82\u2192| `Archived`   | Finalized. No further state transitions possible.                                         |\n    83\u2192\n    84\u2192### 3.2 \u2011 Transition Rules\n    85\u2192\n    86\u21921. `Freeze` requires multi-sig approval by **creator + \u226551 % current holders**.\n    87\u21922. `Inspire` requires PoI-selected composer **+ gRPC verification**.\n    88\u21923. `Evolve*` may only occur once every _epoch_ (`config.evolution_cadence`).\n    89\u21924. `Merge` requires `Fragmented` tokens to reference the same `origin_hash`.\n    90\u21925. `Burn` is irreversible and must pass the runtime `BurnPolicy` strategy.\n    91\u2192\n    92\u2192---\n    93\u2192\n    94\u2192## 4 \u2011 gRPC API (`proto/nft_evolution.proto`)\n    95\u2192\n    96\u2192```proto\n    97\u2192syntax = \"proto3\";\n    98\u2192\n    99\u2192package canvaschain.nft.v1;\n   100\u2192\n   101\u2192service Evolution {\n   102\u2192  rpc Inspire(InspireRequest) returns (InspireResponse);\n   103\u2192  rpc Freeze(FreezeRequest)   returns (FreezeResponse);\n   104\u2192  rpc Evolve(EvolveRequest)   returns (EvolveResponse);\n   105\u2192  rpc Split(SplitRequest)     returns (SplitResponse);\n   106\u2192  rpc Merge(MergeRequest)     returns (MergeResponse);\n   107\u2192  rpc Burn(BurnRequest)       returns (BurnResponse);\n   108\u2192}\n   109\u2192\n   110\u2192message InspireRequest  { string nft_id = 1; bytes vrf_proof = 2; }\n   111\u2192message InspireResponse { bool   accepted = 1; }\n   112\u2192\n   113\u2192message FreezeRequest   { string nft_id = 1; repeated string signatures = 2; }\n   114\u2192message FreezeResponse  { bool   accepted = 1; }\n   115\u2192\n   116\u2192message EvolveRequest   { string nft_id = 1; bytes patch = 2; }\n   117\u2192message EvolveResponse  { string new_cid = 1; }\n   118\u2192\n   119\u2192message SplitRequest    { string nft_id = 1; uint32 parts = 2; }\n   120\u2192message SplitResponse   { repeated string child_ids = 1; }\n   121\u2192\n   122\u2192message MergeRequest    { repeated string child_ids = 1; }\n   123\u2192message MergeResponse   { string merged_id = 1; }\n   124\u2192\n   125\u2192message BurnRequest     { string nft_id = 1; }\n   126\u2192message BurnResponse    { bool burned = 1; }\n   127\u2192```\n   128\u2192\n   129\u2192---\n   130\u2192\n   131\u2192## 5 \u2011 Rust Reference Implementation (core excerpt)\n   132\u2192\n   133\u2192```rust\n   134\u2192//! nft_runtime/src/state_machine.rs\n   135\u2192use crate::error::NftError;\n   136\u2192use chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\n   137\u2192use serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\n   138\u2192\n   139\u2192#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize, PartialEq, Eq)]\n   140\u2192pub enum Phase {\n   141\u2192    Seeded,\n   142\u2192    Dormant,\n   143\u2192    Flourishing,\n   144\u2192    Fragmented,\n   145\u2192    Archived,\n   146\u2192}\n   147\u2192\n   148\u2192#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n   149\u2192pub struct EvolutionEvent {\n   150\u2192    pub nft_id: String,\n   151\u2192    pub from: Phase,\n   152\u2192    pub to: Phase,\n   153\u2192    pub tx_hash: String,\n   154\u2192    pub timestamp: DateTime<Utc>,\n   155\u2192}\n   156\u2192\n   157\u2192impl EvolutionEvent {\n   158\u2192    pub fn sanity_check(&self) -> Result<(), NftError> {\n   159\u2192        if self.from == self.to {\n   160\u2192            return Err(NftError::InvalidTransition(\n   161\u2192                \"from and to phase are identical\".into(),\n   162\u2192            ));\n   163\u2192        }\n   164\u2192        Ok(())\n   165\u2192    }\n   166\u2192}\n   167\u2192\n   168\u2192pub trait Evolvable {\n   169\u2192    fn current_phase(&self) -> Phase;\n   170\u2192    fn transition(&mut self, to: Phase) -> Result<EvolutionEvent, NftError>;\n   171\u2192}\n   172\u2192\n   173\u2192impl Evolvable for Nft {\n   174\u2192    fn current_phase(&self) -> Phase {\n   175\u2192        self.phase.clone()\n   176\u2192    }\n   177\u2192\n   178\u2192    fn transition(&mut self, to: Phase) -> Result<EvolutionEvent, NftError> {\n   179\u2192        ensure_transition_is_valid(self.phase.clone(), to.clone())?;\n   180\u2192        let event = EvolutionEvent {\n   181\u2192            nft_id: self.id.clone(),\n   182\u2192            from: self.phase.clone(),\n   183\u2192            to: to.clone(),\n   184\u2192            tx_hash: blake3::hash(self.id.as_bytes()).to_string(),\n   185\u2192            timestamp: Utc::now(),\n   186\u2192        };\n   187\u2192        event.sanity_check()?;\n   188\u2192        self.phase = to;\n   189\u2192        Ok(event)\n   190\u2192    }\n   191\u2192}\n   192\u2192\n   193\u2192fn ensure_transition_is_valid(from: Phase, to: Phase) -> Result<(), NftError> {\n   194\u2192    use Phase::*;\n   195\u2192    match (from, to) {\n   196\u2192        (Seeded, Dormant)\n   197\u2192        | (Dormant, Flourishing)\n   198\u2192        | (Flourishing, Flourishing)\n   199\u2192        | (Flourishing, Fragmented)\n   200\u2192        | (Fragmented, Dormant)\n   201\u2192        | (Flourishing, Archived)\n   202\u2192        | (Dormant, Archived) => Ok(()),\n   203\u2192\n   204\u2192        _ => Err(NftError::InvalidTransition(format!(\n   205\u2192            \"illegal transition {:?} \u2192 {:?}\",\n   206\u2192            from, to\n   207\u2192        ))),\n   208\u2192    }\n   209\u2192}\n   210\u2192```\n   211\u2192\n   212\u2192_Error definitions omitted; see `error.rs`._\n   213\u2192\n   214\u2192---\n   215\u2192\n   216\u2192## 6 \u2011 Event-Driven Flow\n   217\u2192\n   218\u21921. *Client* signs and submits `EvolveRequest`.\n   219\u21922. **NFT Runtime Svc** validates patch and calls `Nft::transition(Flourishing)`.\n   220\u21923. Upon success it publishes:\n   221\u2192\n   222\u2192```json\n   223\u2192{\n   224\u2192  \"topic\": \"canvaschain.nft.evolved\",\n   225\u2192  \"payload\": {\n   226\u2192    \"nft_id\": \"0xA11CE\",\n   227\u2192    \"new_cid\": \"bafybeia...\",\n   228\u2192    \"epoch\": 1192\n   229\u2192  }\n   230\u2192}\n   231\u2192```\n   232\u2192\n   233\u21924. **Observer UI** receives the event via WebSocket bridge and performs a live\n   234\u2192   transition animation, fetching the new asset layer from IPFS.\n   235\u2192\n   236\u2192---\n   237\u2192\n   238\u2192## 7 \u2011 Strategy-Based Burn Policy (pluggable)\n   239\u2192\n   240\u2192```rust\n   241\u2192pub trait BurnPolicy: Send + Sync {\n   242\u2192    fn can_burn(&self, nft: &Nft, requester: &Address) -> bool;\n   243\u2192}\n   244\u2192\n   245\u2192pub struct SimpleBurn;\n   246\u2192impl BurnPolicy for SimpleBurn {\n   247\u2192    fn can_burn(&self, nft: &Nft, requester: &Address) -> bool {\n   248\u2192        nft.creator == *requester\n   249\u2192    }\n   250\u2192}\n   251\u2192\n   252\u2192pub struct GovernanceBurn {\n   253\u2192    pub quorum: u8,\n   254\u2192}\n   255\u2192impl BurnPolicy for GovernanceBurn {\n   256\u2192    fn can_burn(&self, nft: &Nft, _requester: &Address) -> bool {\n   257\u2192        dao::current_support(nft.id()) >= self.quorum\n   258\u2192    }\n   259\u2192}\n   260\u2192```\n   261\u2192\n   262\u2192The active strategy is selected at runtime through a *chain spec* parameter,\n   263\u2192enabling experimental collectives to upgrade without a hard-fork.\n   264\u2192\n   265\u2192---\n   266\u2192\n   267\u2192## 8 \u2011 Edge Cases & Error Handling\n   268\u2192\n   269\u2192| Case                         | Response                                   |\n   270\u2192|------------------------------|--------------------------------------------|\n   271\u2192| Transition during lock       | `LOCKED` gRPC status.                     |\n   272\u2192| Epoch cadence violation      | `FAILED_PRECONDITION` with retry-after.    |\n   273\u2192| Missing VRF proof on Inspire | `UNAUTHENTICATED`.                         |\n   274\u2192| Merge with mismatched DNA    | `INVALID_ARGUMENT`.                        |\n   275\u2192\n   276\u2192---\n   277\u2192\n   278\u2192## 9 \u2011 Migration Notes (v0.9 \u2192 v1.0)\n   279\u2192\n   280\u21921. `Paused` state removed; use `Dormant`.\n   281\u21922. `Evolve` cadence changed to epoch-based (was block-based).\n   282\u21923. `Split` now returns deterministic `child_ids` derived from "     1\u2192```markdown\n     2\u2192# CanvasChain Symphony \u2013 Proof-of-Inspiration (PoI) Consensus  \n     3\u2192*Version 1.3 \u2013 Status: **Draft-Stable***  \n     4\u2192\n     5\u2192---\n     6\u2192\n     7\u2192## 1  Overview\n     8\u2192Proof-of-Inspiration (PoI) is CanvasChain Symphony\u2019s bespoke, stake-weighted, VRF-driven consensus that empowers **composer nodes** to publish on-chain creative updates (\u201cmovements\u201d).  \n     9\u2192PoI combines:\n    10\u2192\n    11\u2192* **Delegated Proof-of-Stake (DPoS)** \u2013 capital-efficient security and democratic representation.  \n    12\u2192* **Verifiable Random Functions (VRF)** \u2013 unbiased, publicly verifiable randomness to \u2200 participants.  \n    13\u2192* **On-chain Inspiration Score** \u2013 dynamic modifier fueled by historical creative performance, rewarding nodes that consistently contribute high-value artwork.\n    14\u2192\n    15\u2192The result is a fast-finality, low-energy, creative-centric protocol optimized for **interactive NFT evolution**.\n    16\u2192\n    17\u2192---\n    18\u2192\n    19\u2192## 2  Design Goals\n    20\u2192\n    21\u2192| Goal                   | Rationale                                               |\n    22\u2192|------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------|\n    23\u2192| Deterministic yet unpredictable leader election | Prevent censorship & ensure fairness. |\n    24\u2192| Human-readable on-chain proofs                 | Facilitate curator audits & gallery integrations. |\n    25\u2192| Upgrade-friendly crypto curves (Strategy Pattern) | Support Ed25519, BLS12-381, PQC curves. |\n    26\u2192| Slashing for inactivity or malicious art spam | Maintain network & aesthetic integrity. |\n    27\u2192\n    28\u2192---\n    29\u2192\n    30\u2192## 3  Terminology\n    31\u2192\n    32\u2192| Term               | Meaning                                                             |\n    33\u2192|--------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------|\n    34\u2192| Composer Node      | Validator eligible to mint a **Movement Block** during a round.     |\n    35\u2192| Stake Pool         | Set of delegators backing a validator\u2019s stake.                      |\n    36\u2192| Inspiration Score  | Exponential moving average of community upvotes on past work.      |\n    37\u2192| Movement Block     | L2 block holding multi-layer NFT diffs + governance meta.           |\n    38\u2192| Epoch              | 4 960 blocks (\u2248 24 h) after which stake snapshots & rewards settle. |\n    39\u2192| Round              | Smallest consensus unit \u2013 one Movement Block opportunity.          |\n    40\u2192\n    41\u2192---\n    42\u2192\n    43\u2192## 4  Stake Weighting Formula\n    44\u2192\n    45\u2192```\n    46\u2192effective_stake(v) =\n    47\u2192    base_stake(v) +\n    48\u2192    \u03a3 delegator_balances(v)  \u00d7  loyalty_multiplier(d) +\n    49\u2192    inspiration_score(v) \u00d7 \u03b2\n    50\u2192```\n    51\u2192\n    52\u2192*`\u03b2` is set by governance (default 1 \u2030 of total supply).  \n    53\u2192*Loyalty multiplier is 1.0 \u2192 1.2 based on delegation age.*\n    54\u2192\n    55\u2192---\n    56\u2192\n    57\u2192## 5  VRF-Based Composer Selection\n    58\u2192\n    59\u2192Each validator performs:\n    60\u2192\n    61\u21921. Compute `seed = H(epoch_randomness \u2016 round_no)`.\n    62\u21922. Evaluate `vrf_out, vrf_proof = VRF_sk(seed)`.\n    63\u21923. Calculate `threshold = 2^256 \u00d7 effective_stake / total_effective_stake`.\n    64\u21924. If `vrf_out < threshold` \u2192 **win** composer slot.\n    65\u2192\n    66\u2192Because `vrf_out` is \u2208 [0,2\u00b2\u2075\u2076), the probability of winning is proportional to stake.  \n    67\u2192The `vrf_proof` is gossiped with the candidate Movement Block allowing any node to verify:\n    68\u2192\n    69\u2192```rust\n    70\u2192pub fn verify_candidate(\n    71\u2192    pk: &PublicKey,\n    72\u2192    proof: &VrfProof,\n    73\u2192    seed: &[u8; 32],\n    74\u2192    threshold: U256,\n    75\u2192) -> bool {\n    76\u2192    match pk.verify_vrf(seed, proof) {\n    77\u2192        Ok(vrf_out) => U256::from_big_endian(&vrf_out) < threshold,\n    78\u2192        Err(_) => false,\n    79\u2192    }\n    80\u2192}\n    81\u2192```\n    82\u2192\n    83\u2192The Strategy Pattern enables drop-in `verify_vrf` impls for *Ed25519-Dalek*, *blst*, or future PQC curves.\n    84\u2192\n    85\u2192---\n    86\u2192\n    87\u2192## 6  Round Lifecycle\n    88\u2192\n    89\u2192```mermaid\n    90\u2192sequenceDiagram\n    91\u2192    participant V as Validator\n    92\u2192    participant P as PeerValidators\n    93\u2192    participant EB as EventBus(gRPC)\n    94\u2192    V->>V: Generate VRF proof\n    95\u2192    V-->>P: Gossip { Movement Block, vrf_proof }\n    96\u2192    P->>P: Verify vrf, check stake threshold\n    97\u2192    P-->>EB: Emit RoundValidated\n    98\u2192    EB-->>SmartContracts: Relay NFT diffs\n    99\u2192    EB-->>Wallets: Stream ownership events\n   100\u2192```\n   101\u2192\n   102\u21921. **VRF Generation** \u2013 Validators lock in their intent \u2264 400 ms.  \n   103\u21922. **Proposal Gossip** \u2013 Only one valid Movement Block per round is accepted.  \n   104\u21923. **Fast Finality** \u2013 BFT pre-vote + pre-commit (< 2 s).  \n   105\u21924. **Event Hooks** \u2013 Once finalized, the Event Bus notifies microservices.  \n   106\u2192\n   107\u2192---\n   108\u2192\n   109\u2192## 7  Slashing & Rewards\n   110\u2192\n   111\u2192| Violation                     | Penalty                         |\n   112\u2192|-------------------------------|---------------------------------|\n   113\u2192| Double Movement (same round)  | 5 % stake slash + freeze 1 epoch |\n   114\u2192| Invalid VRF proof             | 100 % block reward burned       |\n   115\u2192| Inactivity \u2265 256 rounds       | 1 % stake slash                 |\n   116\u2192\n   117\u2192Block rewards are split:\n   118\u2192\n   119\u2192* 90 % \u2192 Composer + delegators (pro-rata)  \n   120\u2192* 10 % \u2192 Inspiration Fund for community grants  \n   121\u2192\n   122\u2192---\n   123\u2192\n   124\u2192## 8  Reference Rust Implementation Snippet\n   125\u2192\n   126\u2192```rust\n   127\u2192//! PoI core engine \u2013 extracts domain logic, free of networking details.\n   128\u2192\n   129\u2192use crate::crypto::{CurveKind, VrfKeypair};\n   130\u2192use crate::staking::{StakeLedger, InspirationRegistry};\n   131\u2192use crate::types::{EpochRandomness, RoundNumber, MovementBlock};\n   132\u2192use anyhow::{anyhow, Result};\n   133\u2192use uint::construct_uint;\n   134\u2192\n   135\u2192construct_uint! {\n   136\u2192    /// 256-bit unsigned integer.\n   137\u2192    pub struct U256(4);\n   138\u2192}\n   139\u2192\n   140\u2192pub struct ComposerSelector<'a> {\n   141\u2192    stake_ledger: &'a StakeLedger,\n   142\u2192    inspiration:  &'a InspirationRegistry,\n   143\u2192    curve:        CurveKind,\n   144\u2192}\n   145\u2192\n   146\u2192impl<'a> ComposerSelector<'a> {\n   147\u2192    pub fn new(\n   148\u2192        stake_ledger: &'a StakeLedger,\n   149\u2192        inspiration:  &'a InspirationRegistry,\n   150\u2192        curve:        CurveKind,\n   151\u2192    ) -> Self {\n   152\u2192        Self { stake_ledger, inspiration, curve }\n   153\u2192    }\n   154\u2192\n   155\u2192    /// Determine whether `keypair` is eligible to compose `round`.\n   156\u2192    pub fn evaluate(\n   157\u2192        &self,\n   158\u2192        keypair: &VrfKeypair,\n   159\u2192        epoch_rand: &EpochRandomness,\n   160\u2192        round: RoundNumber,\n   161\u2192    ) -> Result<Option<(U256 /*vrf_out*/, Vec<u8> /*proof*/)>> {\n   162\u2192        // 1. Build seed\n   163\u2192        let seed = blake3::hash(&[epoch_rand.as_ref(), &round.to_le_bytes()].concat());\n   164\u2192        // 2. Evaluate VRF\n   165\u2192        let (vrf_out, proof) = keypair\n   166\u2192            .vrf_sign(&seed.as_bytes())\n   167\u2192            .map_err(|e| anyhow!(\"vrf error: {e}\"))?;\n   168\u2192        // 3. Compute threshold\n   169\u2192        let effective = self.stake_ledger.effective_stake(&keypair.public)?;\n   170\u2192        let total    = self.stake_ledger.total_effective_stake();\n   171\u2192        if total.is_zero() {\n   172\u2192            return Err(anyhow!(\"total stake is zero\"));\n   173\u2192        }\n   174\u2192        let threshold = (U256::MAX / total) * effective; // proportional.\n   175\u2192        // 4. Decide\n   176\u2192        let out = U256::from_big_endian(&vrf_out);\n   177\u2192        if out < threshold {\n   178\u2192            Ok(Some((out, proof)))\n   179\u2192        } else {\n   180\u2192            Ok(None)\n   181\u2192        }\n   182\u2192    }\n   183\u2192}\n   184\u2192```\n   185\u2192\n   186\u2192The snippet is dependency-free (besides `blake3`, `uint`, `anyhow`) and demonstrates Strategy-enabled `CurveKind`.\n   187\u2192\n   188\u2192---\n   189\u2192\n   190\u2192## 9  Integration Touch-Points\n   191\u2192\n   192\u21921. **gRPC Service** `composer.proto` \u2013 publishes `SubmitMovement(Block, Proof)` RPC.  \n   193\u21922. **Event Bus Topics**  \n   194\u2192   \u2022 `movement.finalized` \u2013 L2 block header.  \n   195\u2192   \u2022 `staking.slash`      \u2013 Slashing verdicts.  \n   196\u21923. **Smart-Contract Hooks**  \n   197\u2192   \u2022 `on_movement()` \u2013 Allow NFTs to react to fresh traits.  \n   198\u2192\n   199\u2192---\n   200\u2192\n   201\u2192## 10  Future Work\n   202\u2192\n   203\u2192* **MEV-Resistant Inspiration Auctions** \u2013 experimental.  \n   204\u2192* **Composable ZK-VRF** \u2013 hide stake amounts while preserving verifiability.  \n   205\u2192* **PQC Migration Path** \u2013 NIST finalist lattice-based VRF.\n   206\u2192\n   207\u2192---\n   208\u2192\n   209\u2192## 11  Glossary\n   210\u2192\n   211\u2192* **Movement** \u2013 incremental state diff of a multilayer NFT.  \n   212\u2192* **Inspiration Fund** \u2013 treasury for artists, seeded by protocol inflation.  \n   213\u2192* **Strategy Pattern** \u2013 runtime-selectable cryptographic backend.\n   214\u2192\n   215\u2192---\n   216\u2192\n   217\u2192\u00a9 2024 CanvasChain Contributors \u2013 Licensed under Apache-2.0\n   218\u2192```\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. 31337\n   136\u2192\n   137\u2192[postgres]\n   138\u2192dsn = \"postgres://canvas:canvas@localhost:5432/canvas_nft\"\n   139\u2192\n   140\u2192[crypto]\n   141\u2192curve = \"ed25519\" # ed25519 | 148\u2192## 8   Code Walk-Through\n   149\u2192\n   150\u2192```rust\n   151\u2192//! cmd/minting_service/main.rs\n   152\u2192#![forbid(unsafe_code)]\n   153\u2192use minting_service::{config::Config, server::MintingServer};\n   154\u2192use anyhow::Result;\n   155\u2192use tracing::{info, error};\n   156\u2192use tracing_subscriber::EnvFilter;\n   157\u2192\n   158\u2192#[tokio::main]\n   159\u2192async fn main() -> Result<()> {\n   160\u2192    // Initialise logging\n   161\u2192    tracing_subscriber::fmt()\n   162\u2192        .with_env_filter(EnvFilter::from_default_env())\n   163\u2192        .init();\n   164\u2192\n   165\u2192    // Load configuration\n   166\u2192    let cfg = Config::from_env()?;\n   167\u2192 \"MintingService terminated with error\");\n   172\u2192        std::process::exit(1);\n   173\u2192    }\n   174\u2192    Ok(())\n   175\u2192}\n   176\u2192```\n   177\u2192\n   178\u2192Highlights:\n   179\u2192\n   180\u2192* `Strategy Pattern` \u2013 `crypto::Signer` trait with curve-specific back-ends (Ed25519/BLS/\u2026)\n   181\u2192* `Proxy Pattern` \u2013 contract factory `Factory<x>::deploy_proxy(\u2026)`\n   182\u2192* `Event Driven` \u2013 `EventPublisher` & `EventSubscriber` interfaces over `async_nats`\n   183\u2192* `State Machine` \u2013 `MintJobState` (Queued \u2192 PendingTx \u2192 Confirmed | Failed)\n   184\u2192\n   185\u2192---\n   186\u2192\n   187\u2192## 9   Error Semantics\n   188\u2192\n   189\u2192| gRPC code | Meaning                        | Retry |\n   190\u2192| --------- | ----------------------------- | ----- |\n   191\u2192| `INVALID_ARGUMENT` | Bad input (metadata URI missing, royalty > 100%) | No |\n   192\u2192| `UNAUTHENTICATED`  | Invalid artist signature / expired nonce         | No |\n   193\u2192| `RESOURCE_EXHAUSTED` | Rate limit exceeded (composer node)          | Yes, after `Retry-After` header |\n   194\u2192| `INTERNAL`         | Unexpected error, check `error_id`              | Maybe |\n   195\u2192\n   196\u2192A structured error (`ErrorBody`) is serialized in `details`.\n   197\u2192\n   198\u2192---\n   199\u2192\n   200\u2192## 10   Observability\n   201\u2192\n   202\u2192* **Metrics** \u2013 `OpenTelemetry` exporter (`/metrics` Prometheus scrape)  \n   203\u2192* **Tracing** default, switch to pretty with `RUST_LOG_STYLE=pretty`\n   206\u2192\n   207\u2192---\n   208\u2192\n   209\u2192## 11   Extending the Service\n   210\u2192\n   211\u2192* Add new crypto curves by implementing `crypto::Signer` + registering in `crypto::registry`.\n   212\u2192* Support new NFT standards (e.g., ERC-3525) via the `contract::factory` module.\n   213\u2192* Custom throttling "     1\u2192```markdown\n     2\u2192# CanvasChain Symphony \u2013 Marketplace Service\n     3\u2192`services/marketplace_service`\n     4\u2192\n     5\u2192The Marketplace Service powers the primary and secondary exchange of multilayer NFTs\n     6\u2192(\u201cInstruments\u201d) on CanvasChain Symphony.  It exposes a gRPC interface for listing,\n     7\u2192bidding, buying, and royalty-settlement, publishes domain events on the mesh-bus,\n     8\u2192and persists state changes in PostgreSQL using Diesel.  \n     9\u2192The service is designed to be **stateless**; business state is maintained in the\n    10\u2192database and propagated through events.  \n    11\u2192High-throughput order-matching is achieved with an _in-memory order-book_ backed\n    12\u2192by **MVCC snapshots** so reads never block writes.\n    13\u2192\n    14\u2192---\n    15\u2192\n    16\u2192## Table of Contents\n    17\u21921. 64\u2192## 3. gRPC Service Definition\n    65\u2192```proto\n    66\u2192// proto/marketplace.proto\n    67\u2192syntax = \"proto3\";\n    68\u2192package canvas.marketplace;\n    69\u2192\n Integration Test Example\n   214\u2192```rust\n   215\u2192#[tokio::test]\n   216\u2192async fn it_lists_and_buys() {\n   217\u2192    let mut client = MarketplaceClient::connect(\"http://[::1]:6001\").await.unwrap();\n   218\u2192\n   219\u2192    // 1. List an NFT\n   220\u2192    let list_res = client.list_instrument(ListInstrumentRequest {\n   221\u2192        instrument_id: Uuid::new_v4().to_string(),\n   222\u2192        price_microunit: 1_000_000u64,\n   223\u2192        expiration_secs: 86_400,\n   224\u2192    }).await.unwrap().into_inner();\n   225\u2192\n   226\u2192    // 2. Buy it\n   227\u2192    let buy_res = client.buy_instrument(BuyInstrumentRequest {\n   228\u2192        listing_id: list_res.listing_id,\n   229\u2192        buyer_wallet: \"wallet1p5...\".into(),\n   230\u2192    }).await.unwrap().into_inner();\n   231\u2192\n   232\u2192    assert!(buy_res.tx_hash.starts_with(\"0x\"));\n   233\u2192}\n   234\u2192```\n   235\u2192\n   236\u2192Run with:\n   237\u2192```bash\n   238\u2192cargo test -p marketplace_service -- --nocapture\n   239\u2192```\n   240\u2192\n   241\u2192---\n   242\u2192\n   243\u2192## 10. Extending / Plug-Ins\n   244\u2192The Marketplace leverages the **Strategy Pattern** for _fee calculation_:\n   245\u2192\n   246\u2192```rust\n   247\u2192pub trait FeePolicy: Send + Sync {\n   248\u2192    fn taker_fee(&self, price: &BigDecimal) -> BigDecimal;\n   249\u2192    fn maker_fee(&self, price: &BigDecimal) -> BigDecimal;\n   250\u2192}\n   251\u2192\n   252\u2192pub struct FlatFee {\n   253\u2192    pub bps: u32 // basis points, e.g. 25 = 0.25%\n   254\u2192}\n   255\u2192\n   256\u2192impl FeePolicy for FlatFee {\n   257\u2192    fn taker_fee(&self, price: &BigDecimal) -> BigDecimal {\n   258\u2192        price * BigDecimal::from(self.bps) / BigDecimal::from(10_000u32)\n   259\u2192    }\n   260\u2192    fn maker_fee(&self, price: &BigDecimal) -> BigDecimal { BigDecimal::zero() }\n   261\u2192}\n   262\u2192```\n   263\u2192Drop your own policy in `src/fees/` and register via Rocket\u2019s `Figment` or\n   264\u2192`feature = \"dynamic-fees\"`.\n   265\u2192\n   266\u2192---\n   267\u2192\n   268\u2192## 11. Troubleshooting & FAQ\n   269\u2192Q: _\u201cI\u2019m seeing `deadlock detected` errors in logs\u201d_  \n   270\u2192A: Ensure you are on PostgreSQL \u2265 14.2; the advisory lock upgrade reduces deadlocks\n   271\u2192in high-concurrency auctions.\n   272\u2192\n   273\u2192Q: _\u201cEvents are not replaying on cold start\u201d_  \n   274\u2192A: Verify `JetStream` stream `marketplace.*` is configured with `max_msgs=-1` and\n   275\u2192`retention=workqueue`.\n   276\u2192\n   277\u2192---\n   278\u2192\n   279\u2192\u00a9 2024 CanvasChain Foundation \u2013 Licensed under Apache-2.0\n   280\u2192```\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. "     1\u2192# CanvasChain Symphony \u2013 Node Service\n     2\u2192\n     3\u2192The **Node Service** is the beating heart of CanvasChain Symphony.  \n     4\u2192It encapsulates networking, consensus, state-replication, and provides an ergonomic Rust SDK so higher-level micro-services (composition, remixing, marketplace, etc.) can publish transactions or subscribe to real-time events without re-implementing blockchain plumbing.\n     5\u2192\n     6\u2192---\n     7\u2192\n     8\u2192## \ud83e\udde9 Responsibilities\n     9\u2192\n    10\u21921. Peer-to-peer networking (libp2p over QUIC + noise)\n    11\u21922. Proof-of-Inspiration (PoI) leader election\n    12\u21923. Transaction / block propagation\n    13\u21924. State\u2013machine replication (+ snapshotting)\n    14\u21925. gRPC fa\u00e7ade exposing high-level APIs to the remaining micro-services\n    15\u21926. Event bus bridge (NATS) to fan-out new blocks & governance votes\n    16\u2192\n    17\u2192---\n    18\u2192\n    19\u2192## \ud83d\udd16 Feature Flags\n    20\u2192\n    21\u2192| Cargo Feature            | Description                                |\n    22\u2192|--------------------------|--------------------------------------------|\n    23\u2192| `in-memory-db`           | Use an ephemeral   31\u2192```\n    32\u2192\n    33\u2192---\n    34\u2192\n    35\u2192## \ud83d\uddc4\ufe0f Directory Layout\n    36\u2192\n    37\u2192```\n    38\u2192services/node_service\n Binary entry-point\n    53\u2192\u2514\u2500\u2500 README.md                 # You are here\n    54\u2192```\n    55\u2192\n    56\u2192---\n    57\u2192\n    58\u2192## \u2699\ufe0f Configuration\n using `tonic_build`.\n    93\u2192\n    94\u2192Example service snippet (simplified):\n    95\u2192\n    96\u2192```proto\n    97\u2192service CanvasNode {\n    98\u2192  rpc SubmitTransaction (SignedTransaction) returns (TxReceipt);\n    99\u2192  rpc GetBlockByHash     (BlockHash)        returns (Block);\n   100\u2192  rpc SubscribeEvents    (EventFilter)      returns (stream Event);\n   101\u2192}\n   102\u2192```\n   103\u2192\n   104\u2192### Error Model\n   105\u2192\n   106\u2192Errors map to canonical gRPC codes:\n   107\u2192\n   108\u2192| gRPC Code | Meaning                                    |\n   109\u2192|-----------|--------------------------------------------|\n   110\u2192| `INVALID_ARGUMENT` | Input failed schema or signature validation |\n   111\u2192| `UNAVAILABLE`      | Not currently the leader / syncing |\n   112\u2192| `FAILED_PRECONDITION` | Consensus rejected the tx (e.g. nonce) |\n   113\u2192| `INTERNAL`         | Unexpected panic \u2192 logged + Sentry |\n   114\u2192\n   115\u2192---\n   116\u2192\n   117\u2192## \ud83d\ude80 Quick Start\n   118\u2192\n   119\u2192```bash\n   120\u2192# 1. Clone repo\n   121\u2192git clone https://github.com/canvaschain/symphony.git\n   122\u2192cd symphony/services/node_service\n   123\u2192\n   124\u2192# 2. Build with default Ed25519 curve\n   125\u2192cargo build --release\n   126\u2192\n   127\u2192# 3. Generate keys (stored in ./keys/)\n   128\u2192cargo run --bin keygen ed25519\n   129\u2192\n   130\u2192# 4. Run a standalone dev-node with an in-memory DB and verbose logs\n   131\u2192RUST_LOG=debug cargo run --features in-memory-db\n   132\u2192```\n   133\u2192\n   134\u2192---\n   135\u2192\n   136\u2192## \ud83e\uddd1\u200d\ud83d\udcbb Embedding the SDK\n   137\u2192\n   138\u2192Use the SDK in another micro-service (e.g. composition_service):\n   139\u2192\n   140\u2192```toml\n   141\u2192[dependencies]\n   142\u2192canvas_node_sdk = { path = \"../services/node_service\", default-features = false }\n   143\u2192prost = \"0.12\"\n   144\u2192tonic = { version = \"0.10\", features=[\"transport\"] }\n   145\u2192```\n   146\u2192\n   147\u2192```rust\n   148\u2192use canvas_node_sdk::grpc::canvas_node_client::CanvasNodeClient;\n   149\u2192use tonic::transport::Channel;\n   150\u2192\n   151\u2192#[tokio::main]\n   152\u2192async fn main() -> Result<(), Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {\n   153\u2192    let mut client = CanvasNodeClient::connect(\"http://localhost:50051\").await?;\n   154\u2192\n   155\u2192    let tx = build_artist_transaction();\n   156\u2192    let receipt = client.submit_transaction(tx).await?.into_inner();\n   157\u2192\n   158\u2192    println!(\"\ud83c\udf89 Mined in block {}\", receipt.block_number);\n   159\u2192    Ok(())\n   160\u2192}\n   161\u2192```\n   162\u2192\n   163\u2192---\n   164\u2192\n   165\u2192## \ud83c\udfdb\ufe0f Consensus in 60 Seconds\n   166\u2192\n   167\u21921. Epoch is fixed (#blocks = `epoch_duration_sec / slot_time_sec`)\n   168\u21922. VRF leader randomness is derived from last block hash + validator stake\n   169\u21923. Committee = top-N validators by stake (configurable)\n   170\u21924. Fork-choice = GHOST for liveness; blocks must include VRF proof\n   171\u21925. Finality via BFT overlay (HotStuff variant) after 2 rounds\n   172\u2192\n   173\u2192See `src/consensus/proof_of_inspiration.rs` for full implementation & unit tests.\n   174\u2192\n   175\u2192---\n   176\u2192\n   177\u2192## \ud83d\udcc8 Metrics & Observability\n   178\u2192\n   179\u2192Prometheus exporter is enabled by default at `/metrics` (port 9103).\n   180\u2192\n   181\u2192Key metrics:\n   182\u2192\u2022 `canvas_block_height`\n   183\u2192\u2022 `canvas_peer_count`\n   184\u2192\u2022 `canvas_tx_pool_size`\n   185\u2192\u2022 `canvas_leader_election_duration_seconds`\n   186\u2192\n   187\u2192Enable Jaeger tracing:\n   188\u2192\n   189\u2192```bash\n   190\u2192JAEGER_ENDPOINT=http://localhost:14268/api/traces RUST_LOG=info,tower_http=debug \\\n   191\u2192    cargo run --release\n   192\u2192```\n   193\u2192\n   194\u2192---\n   195\u2192\n   196\u2192## \ud83d\udd12 Security Checklist\n   197\u2192\n   198\u2192- AES-GCM sealed storage for private keys (`KeyVault`)\n   199\u2192- All peer traffic encrypted via Noise_KK\n   200\u2192- Strict Protobuf schema validation (`prost-types` + `schemars`)\n   201\u2192- Comprehensive fuzzing harness: `cargo fuzz run tx_deserialize`\n   202\u2192\n   203\u2192---\n   204\u2192\n   205\u2192## \ud83d\udcdd Contributing\n   206\u2192\n   207\u21921. 211\u2192        pos.amount = Amount::ZERO;\n   212\u2192        pos.status = PositionStatus::Slashed { reason };\n   213\u2192        Ok(pos)\n   214\u2192    }\n   215\u2192}\n   216\u2192```\n amount).map_err(to_status)?;\n   281\u2192            self.repo.insert(&pos).await.map_err(to_status)?;\n   282\u2192\n   283\u2192            Ok(Response::new(StakeResponse {\n   284\u2192                tx_id: pos.id.to_string(),\n   285\u2192                bonded_at: Some(pos.bonded_at.into()),\n   286\u2192            }))\n   287\u2192        }\n   288\u2192        .instrument(span)\n   289\u2192        .await\n   290\u2192    }\n   291\u2192\n   292\u2192    async fn unstake(\n   293\u2192        &self,\n   294\u2192        req: Request<UnstakeRequest>,\n   295\u2192    ) -> Result<Response<UnstakeResponse>, Status> {\n   296\u2192        let span = info_span!(\"unstake\", ?req);\n   297\u2192        async move {\n   298\u2192            let body = req.into_inner();\n   299\u2192            let pos = self.repo.find_active(&body.account_id).await.map_err(to_status)?;\n   300\u2192\n   301\u2192            let updated = self\n   302\u2192                .engine\n   303\u2192                .unbond(pos, Amount::from(body.amount))\n   304\u2192                .map_err(to_status)?;\n   305\u2192            self.repo.update(&updated).await.map_err(to_status)?;\n   306\u2192\n   307\u2192            Ok(Response::new(UnstakeResponse {\n   308\u2192                tx_id: updated.id.to_string(),\n   309\u2192                unbonding_complete_at: match updated.status {\n   310\u2192                    PositionStatus::Unbonding { completes_at } => Some(completes_at.into()),\n   311\u2192                    _ => None,\n   312\u2192                },\n   313\u2192            }))\n   314\u2192        }\n   315\u2192        .instrument(span)\n   316\u2192        .await\n   317\u2192    }\n   318\u2192\n   319\u2192    async fn slash(\n   320\u2192        &self,\n   321\u2192        req: Request<SlashRequest>,\n   322\u2192    ) -> Result<Response<SlashResponse>, Status> {\n   323\u2192        let span = info_span!(\"slash\", ?req);\n   324\u2192        async move {\n   325\u2192            let body = req.into_inner();\n   326\u2192            let pos = self.repo.find_validator(&body.validator_id).await.map_err(to_status)?;\n   327\u2192\n   328\u2192            let updated = self.engine.slash(pos, body.reason).map_err(to_status)?;\n   329\u2192            self.repo.update(&updated).await.map_err(to_status)?;\n   330\u2192\n   331\u2192            Ok(Response::new(SlashResponse {\n   332\u2192                tx_id: updated.id.to_string(),\n   333\u2192            }))\n   334\u2192        }\n   335\u2192        .instrument(span)\n   336\u2192        .await\n   337\u2192    }\n   338\u2192\n   339\u2192    async fn query(\n   340\u2192        &self,\n   341\u2192        req: Request<QueryRequest>,\n   342\u2192    ) -> Result<Response<QueryResponse>, Status> {\n   343\u2192        let span = info_span!(\"query\", ?req);\n   344\u2192        async move {\n   345\u2192            let body = req.into_inner();\n   346\u2192            let positions = self.repo.list_by_account(&body.account_id).await.map_err(to_status)?;\n   347\u2192            let staked = positions.iter().map(|p| p.amount).sum::<Amount>();\n   348\u2192\n   349\u2192            Ok(Response::new(QueryResponse {\n   350\u2192                staked: staked.mantissa() as u64,\n   351\u2192                pending: 0,\n   352\u2192                reward_accum: 0,\n   353\u2192            }))\n   354\u2192        }\n   355\u2192        .instrument(span)\n   356\u2192        .await\n   357\u2192    }\n   358\u2192}\n   359\u2192\n   360\u2192fn bad_uuid(_: uuid::Error) -> Status {\n   361\u2192    Status::invalid_argument(\"bad account_id\")\n   362\u2192}\n   363\u2192\n   364\u2192fn to_status(err: EngineError) -> Status {\n   365\u2192    Status::internal(err.to_string())\n   366\u2192}\n   367\u2192```\n   368\u2192\n   369\u2192---\n   370\u2192## 8. One-Command Quick-Start\n    51\u2192\n    52\u2192Spin up a fully-fledged local cluster:\n    53\u2192\n    54\u2192```bash\n    55\u2192make devnet\n    56\u2192```\n    57\u2192\n    58\u2192`make devnet` performs the following under the hood:\n    59\u2192\n    60\u21921. Exposes:\n    65\u2192   - gRPC: `localhost:50051`\n    66\u2192   - GraphQL: `http://localhost:8080/graphql`\n    67\u2192   - Polkadot-JS UI: `http://localhost:8000`\n    68\u2192\n    69\u2192Stop and remove containers:\n    70\u2192\n    71\u2192```bash\n    72\u2192make down     # or: docker-compose down -v\n    73\u2192```\n    74\u2192\n    75\u2192---\n    76\u2192\n    77\u2192## 4. Manual Build (Non-Docker)\n    78\u2192\n    79\u2192### 4.1 Compile All Binaries\n    80\u2192\n    81\u2192```bash\n    82\u2192cargo build --workspace --release\n    83\u2192```\n    84\u2192\n    85\u2192Artifacts land in `target/release/`.\n    86\u2192\n    87\u2192### 4.2 Launch Core Services\n    88\u2192\n    89\u2192In separate terminals:\n    90\u2192\n    91\u2192```bash\n    92\u2192# \u2460 Blockchain node (Substrate)\n    93\u2192./target/release/canvas-node --dev --tmp --rpc-methods=Unsafe\n    94\u2192\n    95\u2192# \u2461 Event Bus (NATS)\n    96\u2192nats-server -DV\n    97\u2192\n    98\u2192# \u2462 Composer Microservice\n    99\u2192RUST_LOG=info \\\n   100\u2192COMPOSER_NODE_URL=127.0.0.1:9944 \\\n   101\u2192cargo run -p composer --release\n   102\u2192```\n   103\u2192\n   104\u2192Use `just` recipes (`just --list`) for shortcuts.\n   105\u2192\n   106\u2192---\n   107\u2192\n   108\u2192## 5. Regenerating gRPC Stubs\n   109\u2192\n   110\u2192Whenever you modify files under `proto/`:\n   111\u2192\n   112\u2192```bash\n   113\u2192protoc \\\n   114\u2192  --proto_path=proto \\\n   115\u2192  --prost_out=services \\\n   116\u2192  --tonic_out=services \\\n   117\u2192  proto/**/*.proto\n   118\u2192```\n   119\u2192\n   120\u2192Or simply:\n   121\u2192\n   122\u2192```bash\n   123\u2192make proto\n   124\u2192```\n   125\u2192\n   126\u2192The workspace makes heavy use of [tonic-build] with Prost, mapping Protobuf well-known types to `chrono` and `uuid` seamlessly.\n   127\u2192\n   128\u2192---\n   129\u2192\n   130\u2192## 6. End-to-End Smoke Test\n   131\u2192\n   132\u2192```bash\n   133\u2192cargo test --workspace --all-features\n   134\u2192```\n   135\u2192\n   136\u2192Expect output similar to:\n   137\u2192\n   138\u2192```\n   139\u2192running 192 tests\n   140\u2192test composer::tests::mint_flow ... ok\n   141\u2192test defi::tests::apy_math ... ok\n   142\u2192\u2026\n   143\u2192```\n   144\u2192\n   145\u2192---\n   146\u2192\n   147\u2192## 7. Creating & Deploying a Custom NFT Instrument\n   148\u2192\n   149\u2192Below is a minimal factory template:\n   150\u2192\n   151\u2192```rust\n   152\u2192// pallets/instrument-factory/src/lib.rs\n   153\u2192pub struct GlitchSynthFactory;\n   154\u2192\n   155\u2192impl InstrumentFactory for GlitchSynthFactory {\n   156\u2192    fn instantiate(config: InstrumentConfig) -> Result<InstrumentId, DispatchError> {\n   157\u2192        let id = Self::reserve_id()?;\n   158\u2192        <Instruments<T>>::insert(\n   159\u2192            id,\n   160\u2192            Instrument {\n   161\u2192                owner: config.owner,\n   162\u2192                curve: CurveKind::Bls12381,\n   163\u2192                metadata: config.metadata,\n   164\u2192            },\n   165\u2192        );\n   166\u2192        Self::deposit_event(Event::InstrumentCreated { id, owner: config.owner });\n   167\u2192        Ok(id)\n   168\u2192    }\n   169\u2192}\n   170\u2192```\n   171\u2192\n   172\u2192Compile to WASM and deploy:\n   173\u2192\n   174\u2192```bash\n   175\u2192cargo +nightly contract build -p instrument-factory\n   176\u2192canvas-cli wasm deploy \\\n   177\u2192  --wasm target/ink/instrument-factory.wasm \\\n   178\u2192  --rpc-url ws://127.0.0.1:9944 \\\n   179\u2192  --suri //Alice\n   180\u2192```\n   181\u2192\n   182\u2192---\n   183\u2192\n   184\u2192## 8. Advanced: Swapping Cryptographic Strategies\n   185\u2192\n   186\u2192All crypto operations are abstracted behind the `SignatureScheme` trait:\n   187\u2192\n   188\u2192```rust\n   189\u2192pub trait SignatureScheme {\n   190\u2192    type Public;\n   191\u2192    type Private;\n   192\u2192    type Signature;\n   193\u2192    fn sign(msg: &[u8], sk: &Self::Private) -> Self::Signature;\n   194\u2192    fn verify(msg: &[u8], sig: &Self::Signature, pk: &Self::Public) -> bool;\n   195\u2192}\n   196\u2192\n   197\u2192pub enum DefaultScheme {\n   198\u2192    Ed25519,\n   199\u2192}\n   200\u2192\n   201\u2192impl SignatureScheme for DefaultScheme { \u2026 }\n   202\u2192```\n   203\u2192\n   204\u2192Compile-time selection:\n   205\u2192\n   206\u2192```bash\n   207\u2192# Ed25519 (default)\n   208\u2192cargo build --features curve-ed25519\n   209\u2192\n   210\u2192# BLS12-381 (threshold support)\n   211\u2192cargo build --features curve-bls12-381\n   212\u2192\n   213\u2192# XMSS (post-quantum)\n   214\u2192cargo build --features curve-xmss\n   215\u2192```\n   216\u2192\n   217\u2192---\n   218\u2192\n   219\u2192## 9. Environment Variables\n   220\u2192\n   221\u2192| Variable                    | Purpose                                   | Default                |\n   222\u2192|-----------------------------|-------------------------------------------|------------------------|\n   223\u2192| `NODE_RPC_URL`             | Rust node RPC endpoint                    | `ws://localhost:9944` |\n   224\u2192| `COMPOSER_SEED`            | sr25519 seed phrase for composer node     | `//Alice`             |\n   225\u2192| `EVENT_BUS_URL`            | NATS server address                       | `nats://127.0.0.1:4222`|\n   226\u2192| `DATABASE_URL`             | Postgres connection string                | `postgres://canvas:canvas@localhost/canvas` |\n   227\u2192| `RUST_LOG`                 | Log level (`info`, `debug`, `trace`)      | `info`                |\n   228\u2192\n   229\u2192Load via direnv or `.env`:\n   230\u2192\n   231\u2192```dotenv\n   232\u2192NODE_RPC_URL=ws://127.0.0.1:9944\n   233\u2192COMPOSER_SEED=bottom drive obey lake curtain smoke basket hold race lonely fit walk\n   234\u2192RUST_LOG=trace\n   235\u2192```\n   236\u2192\n   237\u2192---\n   238\u2192\n   239\u2192## 10. Troubleshooting\n   240\u2192\n   241\u2192| Symptom                                | Fix |\n   242\u2192|----------------------------------------|-----|\n   243\u2192| `error: linking with cc failed`        | Ensure `libssl-dev` & `clang` are installed |\n   244\u2192| gRPC returns `UNIMPLEMENTED`           | Version mismatch \u2013 regenerate proto stubs |\n   245\u2192| `PoolTimedOut` from `sqlx`             | Increase `MAX_CONNECTIONS` or use psql \u2265 14 |\n   246\u2192| NFT not minting, tx stuck in `Ready`   | Check that `composer` service is elected (see logs) |\n   247\u2192\n   248\u2192---\n   249\u2192\n   250\u2192## 11. Contribution & Code Style\n   251\u2192\n   252\u21921. `rustfmt --check` enforced via CI.\n   253\u21922. Clippy `-D warnings`.\n   254\u21923. Conventional Commits (`feat:`, `fix:`, `chore:`\u2026).\n   255\u2192\n   256\u2192Create feature branches off `develop`, then open PRs targeting `develop`.\n   257\u2192\n   258\u2192---\n   259\u2192\n   260\u2192## 12. Glossary\n   261\u2192\n   262\u2192- **Proof-of-Inspiration:** Hybrid PoS + VRF consensus selecting creatives to push on-chain art updates.\n   263\u2192- **Instrument:** A composable NFT template (e.g., synthesizer, brush stroke engine).\n   264\u2192- **Movement:** Discrete generative art variation emitted by a composer node.\n   265\u2192- **Royalty Stream:** Continuous, time-based payout leveraging Superfluid-like DeFi contracts.\n   266\u2192\n   267\u2192---\n   268\u2192\n   269\u2192Happy hacking \u2014 _unleash your inner composer!_ \ud83c\udfa8\ud83c\udfb6\n   270\u2192```\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. This module purposefully remains *no_std*-friendly (with an opt-in\n//! `std` feature for clients that need heap allocation) so it can be\n//! reused inside on-chain WASM smart contracts as well as off-chain\n//! micro-services.\n//!\n//! Key design goals:\n//! 1. Multi-layer NFTs with independent ownership & royalty streams.\n//! 2. Fine-grained state transitions driven by user interaction,\n//!    governance votes, staking incentives and DeFi metrics.\n//! 3. Pluggable cryptography via Strategy pattern (`SignatureScheme`).\n//!\n//! NOTE: Heavy business logic such as VRF computation or signature\n//! verification lives in dedicated crates (`ccs_cryptography`, \u2026).\n#![cfg_attr(not(feature = \"std\"), no_std)]\n\nextern crate struct WalletAddress(pub String);\n\nimpl Display for WalletAddress {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n        f.write_str(&self.0)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Token amount in Copy, Clone, Debug, Default, PartialEq, Eq, PartialOrd, Ord, Serialize, Deserialize,\n)]\npub struct BasisPoints(u16);\n\nimpl BasisPoints {\n    pub const MAX: u16 = 10_000;\n\n    pub fn new(bp: type PublicKey;\n    type Signature;\n\n    fn verify(\n        pk: &Self::PublicKey,\n        msg: &[u8],\n        sig: &Self::Signature,\n    ) -> bool;\n}\n\n/// High-level NFT error Audio,\n    Haptic,\n    Metadata,\n    Custom(String),\n}\n\n/// Finite state machine for a layer\u2019s lifecycle.\n#[derive(\n    Copy, Clone, Debug, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, Serialize, Deserialize,\n)]\npub enum LayerState {\n    Draft,\n    Active,\n    Frozen,\n    Retired,\n}\n\nimpl LayerState {\n    pub fn can_transition(self, next: LayerState) -> bool {\n        use LayerState::*;\n        matches!(\n            (self, next),\n            (Draft, Active)\n                | (Active, Frozen)\n                | (Active, Retired)\n                | (Frozen, Retired) // irreversible freeze\n        )\n    }\n}\n\n/// Event that may trigger NFT mutations.\n/// This is serialized and sent over the event bus.\n#[derive(Clone, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum EvolutionEvent {\n    /// A wallet interacted with the NFT (likes, remix, \u2026).\n    Interaction {\n        wallet: WalletAddress,\n        payload: alloc::vec::Vec<u8>,\n    },\n\n    /// Snapshot LayerState,\n    pub owner: WalletAddress,\n    pub royalty_bp: BasisPoints,\n    pub created_at: u64,\n    pub last_updated: u64,\n}\n\nimpl NftLayer {\n    pub fn freeze(&mut self) -> Result<(), NftError> {\n        if self.state == LayerState::Frozen {\n            return Ok(());\n        }\n        if self.state.can_transition(LayerState::Frozen) {\n            self.state = LayerState::Frozen;\n            Ok(())\n        } else {\n            Err(NftError::InvalidStateTransition {\n                from: self.state,\n                to: LayerState::Frozen,\n            })\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Transfer ownership, enforcing the layer\u2019s frozen status.\n    pub fn transfer(\n        &mut self,\n        from: &WalletAddress,\n        to: WalletAddress,\n    ) -> Result<(), NftError> {\n        if &self.owner != from {\n            return Err(NftError::OwnershipMismatch {\n                expected: self.owner.clone(),\n                actual: from.clone(),\n            });\n        }\n\n        if self.state == LayerState::Frozen {\n            return Err(NftError::LayerFrozen(self.id));\n        }\n\n        self.owner = to;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n/// Distribution of royalties across multiple stakeholders.\n#[derive(Clone, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct RoyaltySchedule {\n    recipients: BTreeMap<WalletAddress, BasisPoints>,\n}\n\nimpl RoyaltySchedule {\n    /// Build a new schedule. The sum of `BasisPoints` must be \u2264 10k.\n    pub fn new(\n        recipients: BTreeMap<WalletAddress, BasisPoints>,\n    ) -> Result<Self, NftError> {\n        let total: u32 = recipients\n            .values()\n            .map(|bp| bp.as_u16() as u32)\n            .sum();\n        if total > BasisPoints::MAX as u32 {\n            return Err(NftError::RoyaltyOverflow);\n        }\n        Ok(Self { recipients })\n    }\n\n    /// Resolve the royalty amount for each recipient given a sale price.\n    pub fn split(\n        &self,\n        sale_price: TokenAmount,\n    ) -> BTreeMap<WalletAddress, TokenAmount> {\n        self.recipients\n            .iter()\n            .map(|(addr, bp)| {\n                let amount = sale_price * bp.as_u16() as u128\n                    / BasisPoints::MAX as u128;\n                (addr.clone(), amount)\n            })\n            .collect()\n    }\n}\n\n/// Governance parameters per NFT.\n#[derive(Clone, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct GovernancePolicy {\n    pub quorum_bp: BasisPoints,\n    pub super_majority_bp: BasisPoints,\n    pub voting_period: Duration,\n}\n\n/// The main multi-layer NFT object.\n#[derive(Clone, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct MultiLayerNft {\n    pub id: Uuid,\n    pub name: String,\n    pub creator: WalletAddress,\n    pub layers: BTreeMap<Uuid, NftLayer>,\n    pub governance: GovernancePolicy,\n    pub royalties: RoyaltySchedule,\n}\n\nimpl MultiLayerNft {\n    /// Builder pattern entry point.\n    pub fn builder<S: Into<String>>(\n        name: S,\n        creator: WalletAddress,\n    ) -> NftBuilder {\n        NftBuilder::new(name.into(), creator)\n    }\n\n    /// Compute a deterministic content digest of all layers (Merkle root\n    /// is preferable, but we hash a concatenation for simplicity).\n    pub fn digest(&self) -> blake3::Hash {\n        let mut hasher = blake3::Hasher::new();\n        for layer in self.layers.values() {\n            hasher.update(layer.cid.as_bytes());\n        }\n        hasher.finalize()\n    }\n\n    /// Attempt to mutate the NFT based on an external event.\n    pub fn evolve(\n        &mut self,\n        event: EvolutionEvent,\n    ) -> Result<(), NftError> {\n        match event {\n            EvolutionEvent::Interaction { wallet, payload } => {\n                self.handle_interaction(wallet, payload)\n            }\n            EvolutionEvent::Staked {\n                wallet,\n                amount,\n                duration,\n            } => self.handle_stake(wallet, amount, duration),\n            EvolutionEvent::GovernanceResult {\n                proposal_id: _,\n                approve_ratio,\n            } => self.handle_governance(approve_ratio),\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn handle_interaction(\n        &mut self,\n        wallet: WalletAddress,\n        _payload: Vec<u8>,\n    ) -> Result<(), NftError> {\n        // Simple rule: first interaction grants temporary co-ownership\n        // (until frozen) of layer[0] (Visual) if not already owned.\n        if let Some(first_layer) = self.layers.values_mut().next() {\n            if first_layer.state == LayerState::Active\n                && first_layer.owner != wallet\n            {\n                first_layer.owner = wallet;\n            }\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    fn handle_stake(\n        &mut self,\n        _wallet: WalletAddress,\n        amount: TokenAmount,\n        duration: Duration,\n    ) -> Result<(), NftError> {\n        // Increase royalty shares proportionally to stake (toy logic).\n        let bonus_bp = (amount / 1_000_000_000_000_000_000u128) as u16; // 1 ETH == 10 bp\n        let bonus_bp = bonus_bp.min(1000); // cap at +10%\n        let adjusted = BasisPoints::new(bonus_bp)?;\n        // Add a dummy recipient (treasury) with the bonus share.\n        self.royalties.recipients.insert(\n            WalletAddress(\"canvas_treasury\".into()),\n            adjusted,\n        );\n        // Re-balance to avoid overflow (leftover goes to creator).\n        self.normalize_royalties()?;\n        // Freeze if stake duration > 30 days.\n        if duration.as_secs() >= 30 * 24 * 3600 {\n            for layer in self.layers.values_mut() {\n                layer.freeze()?;\n            }\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    fn handle_governance(\n        &mut self,\n        approve_ratio: BasisPoints,\n    ) -> Result<(), NftError> {\n        if approve_ratio.as_u16() >= self.governance.super_majority_bp.as_u16()\n        {\n            // Promote all `Draft` layers to `Active`.\n            for layer in self.layers.values_mut() {\n                if layer.state == LayerState::Draft {\n                    layer.state = LayerState::Active;\n                }\n            }\n            Ok(())\n        } else {\n            Err(NftError::Governance(\n                \"proposal rejected\".to_string(),\n            ))\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn normalize_royalties(&mut self) -> Result<(), NftError> {\n        let total: u32 = self\n            .royalties\n            .recipients\n            .values()\n            .map(|bp| bp.as_u16() as u32)\n            .sum();\n        if total > BasisPoints::MAX as u32 {\n            return Err(NftError::RoyaltyOverflow);\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Transfer a specific layer to a new owner.\n    pub fn transfer_layer(\n        &mut self,\n        layer_id: Uuid,\n        from: &WalletAddress,\n        to: WalletAddress,\n    ) -> Result<(), NftError> {\n        let layer = self\n            .layers\n            .get_mut(&layer_id)\n            .ok_or(NftError::UnknownLayer(layer_id))?;\n        layer.transfer(from, to)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Fluent builder for `MultiLayerNft`.\npub struct NftBuilder {\n    id: Uuid,\n    name: String,\n royalty_bp: BasisPoints,\n    ) -> Self {\n        let layer = NftLayer {\n            id: Uuid::new_v4(),\n            kind,\n            cid: cid.into(),\n            state: initial_state,\n            owner: self.creator.clone(),\n            royalty_bp,\n            created_at: Self::now(),\n            last_updated: Self::now(),\n        };\n        self.layers.insert(layer.id, layer);\n        self\n    }\n\n    pub fn governance_policy(\n        mut self,\n        policy: GovernancePolicy,\n    ) -> Self {\n        self.governance = Some(policy);\n        self\n    }\n\n    pub fn BasisPoints::new(6_600)?,\n            voting_period: Duration::from_secs(7 * 24 * 3600),\n        });\n\n        let royalties = self.royalties.unwrap_or_else(|| {\n            let mut map = BTreeMap::new();\n            map.insert(self.creator.clone(), BasisPoints(1_000)); // 10%\n            RoyaltySchedule { recipients: map }\n        });\n\n        Ok(MultiLayerNft {\n            id: self.id,\n            name: self.name,\n            creator: self.creator,\n            layers: self.layers,\n            governance,\n            royalties,\n        })\n    }\n\n     "content": "```rust\n//! Node service state\u2013machine\n//!\n//! This module implements a hierarchical, asynchronous state-machine that\n//! drives a single CanvasChain Symphony \u201cconductor\u201d (validator / full node).\n//!\n//! The public fa\u00e7ade is [`NodeStateMachine::spawn`].  Callers provide a\n//! configured [`NodeContext`] plus a Tokio `mpsc::Receiver<NodeEvent>` that\n//! represents the node\u2019s inbound event bus.  \n//!\n//! The machine is built around the classic State pattern.  Each state\n//! implements [`State`]\u2014an async callback that receives the next event and\n//! returns a [`Transition`] indicating whether the machine should:\n//!   * stay in the same state\n//!   * transition to a new boxed state\n//!   * perform a graceful shutdown.\n//!\n//! Transitions are **total**; all event/state combinations _must_ resolve to a\n//! `Transition`, preventing undefined behaviour at runtime.\n//!\n//! -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n//! Conventions & best-practices\n//! -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n//! \u2022 Logging is performed with the `tracing` crate (structured, async-aware).  \n//! \u2022 All public types derive `Debug` to make tracing easier.  \n//! \u2022 Errors bubble up using `thiserror::Error` and are logged before causing a\n//!   transition into [`StateError`].  \n//! \u2022 No blocking I/O\u2014everything is fully async.  \n//! \u2022 `#![deny(clippy::unwrap_used)]` ensures we never `.unwrap()` outside of\n//!   tests.  \n//!\n//! -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n//! Example\n//! -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n//! ```no_run\n//! # use tokio::sync::mpsc;\n//! # use canvas_chain_node_service::state_machine::*;\n//! # #[tokio::main]\n//! # async fn main() -> anyhow::Result<()> {\n//! let (tx, rx) = mpsc::channel(128);\n//! let ctx = NodeContext::new(Default::default(), tx.clone());\n//! let handle = NodeStateMachine::spawn(ctx, rx);\n//!\n//! // Send a dummy event\n//! tx.send(NodeEvent::Tick).await?;\n//!\n//! // Wait until the machine exits\n//! handle.await?;\n//! # Ok::<_, anyhow::Error>(())\n//! # }\n//! ```\n\n#![deny(clippy::unwrap_used)]\n\nuse std::time::Duration;\n\nuse async_trait::async_trait;\nuse tokio::{\n    select,\n    sync::mpsc,\n    task::JoinHandle,\n    time::{interval, Interval},\n};\nuse tracing::{debug, error, info, instrument};\n\nuse crate::event_bus::Publish;\nuse crate::network::types::{Block, PeerId};\nuse crate::storage::Database;\n\n// ------------------------------\n// Public facade\n// ------------------------------\n\n/// Spawn a state-machine on the Tokio runtime and return a [`JoinHandle`]\n/// representing its lifecycle.\npub struct NodeStateMachine;\n\nimpl NodeStateMachine {\n    /// Spawns the asynchronous state machine.  The function immediately returns\n    /// a Tokio [`JoinHandle`] that finishes when the machine reaches the\n    /// [`Transition::Shutdown`] transition or the provided `event_rx` closes.\n    pub fn spawn(\n        mut ctx: NodeContext,\n        mut event_rx: mpsc::Receiver<NodeEvent>,\n    ) -> JoinHandle<anyhow::Result<()>> {\n        tokio::spawn(async move {\n            let mut state: Box<dyn State> = Box::<StateBooting>::default();\n\n            // Heart-beat ticker; every state receives `Tick` events.\n            let mut ticker = interval(Duration::from_secs(5));\n\n            loop {\n                select! {\n                    maybe_evt = event_rx.recv() => {\n                        match maybe_evt {\n                            Some(evt) => {\n                                state = dispatch(&mut ctx, state, evt).await?;\n                            }\n                            None => {\n                                info!(\"event stream closed \u2013 shutting node down\");\n                                break;\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n\n                    _ = ticker.tick() => {\n                        state = dispatch(&mut ctx, state, NodeEvent::Tick).await?;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            info!(node_id=%ctx.config.node_id, \"node service terminated\");\n            Ok(())\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n// ------------------------------\n// Context & Events\n// ------------------------------\n\n/// Immutable configuration for a running node.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct NodeConfig {\n    pub node_id: String,\n    pub network_id: String,\n    pub database_url: String,\n    pub is_validator: bool,\n}\n\nimpl Default for NodeConfig {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            node_id: nanoid::nanoid!(),\n            network_id: \"canvas-testnet\".into(),\n            database_url: \"sqlite::memory:\".into(),\n            is_validator: false,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Long-living, shared runtime context passed to every [`State`].\n#[derive(Debug)]\npub struct NodeContext {\n    pub config: NodeConfig,\n    pub db: Database,\n    pub event_tx: mpsc::Sender<NodeEvent>,\n    pub bus: Publish, // Simplified, re-export from crate::event_bus\n}\n\nimpl NodeContext {\n    pub fn new(config: NodeConfig, event_tx: mpsc::Sender<NodeEvent>) -> Self {\n        let db = Database::connect(&config.database_url)\n            .expect(\"infallible for in-memory; otherwise bubble up\");\n\n        Self {\n            config,\n            db,\n            event_tx,\n            bus: Publish::default(),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// All possible events handled by the state machine.\n#[derive(Debug)]\npub enum NodeEvent {\n    /// Periodic internal heart-beat.\n    Tick,\n\n    /// New peer connected\n    PeerConnected(PeerId),\n\n    /// Network broadcast of a new block announcement.\n    BlockReceived(Block),\n\n    /// The consensus engine elected this node the next composer (\u201cvalidator\u201d).\n    ElectedComposer,\n\n    /// Graceful shutdown request.\n    Shutdown,\n}\n\n// ------------------------------\n// State machinery\n// ------------------------------\n\n/// When a [`State`] finishes processing an event it returns a `Transition`\n/// deciding the machine\u2019s next state.\n#[derive(Debug)]\npub enum Transition {\n    /// Remain in the existing state.\n    Stay,\n    /// Replace current state with a new one.\n    Next(Box<dyn State>),\n    /// Terminate the machine.\n    Shutdown,\n}\n\n/// Common interface implemented by *every* node state.\n#[async_trait]\npub trait State: Send {\n    /// Human-readable name of the state (`&'static str` avoids allocations).\n    fn name(&self) -> &'static str;\n\n    /// Process an incoming event. Must return a valid [`Transition`].\n    async fn on_event(\n        &mut self,\n        ctx: &mut NodeContext,\n        event: NodeEvent,\n    ) -> anyhow::Result<Transition>;\n}\n\n// Wrapper that logs state entry / exit\n#[instrument(skip_all, fields(new_state = next.name()))]\nasync fn dispatch(\n    ctx: &mut NodeContext,\n    mut current: Box<dyn State>,\n    evt: NodeEvent,\n) -> anyhow::Result<Box<dyn State>> {\n    debug!(\n        state = current.name(),\n        evt = format!(\"{:?}\", evt),\n        \"handling event\"\n    );\n\n    let transition = match current.on_event(ctx, evt).await {\n        Ok(t) => t,\n        Err(e) => {\n            error!(\"state {:?} returned error: {e:?}\", current.name());\n            return Ok(Box::new(StateError::new(e)));\n        }\n    };\n\n    let next: Box<dyn State> = match transition {\n        Transition::Stay => current,\n        Transition::Next(next_state) => next_state,\n        Transition::Shutdown => {\n            info!(\"shutdown requested by state {}\", current.name());\n            return Err(anyhow::anyhow!(\"state-machine shutdown\"));\n        }\n    };\n\n    Ok(next)\n}\n\n// ------------------------------\n// Concrete States\n// ------------------------------\n\n/// Initial boot / self-check state.\n#[derive(Default)]\nstruct StateBooting;\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl State for StateBooting {\n    fn name(&self) -> &'static str {\n        \"Booting\"\n    }\n\n    #[instrument(skip_all)]\n    async fn on_event(\n        &mut self,\n        ctx: &mut NodeContext,\n        event: NodeEvent,\n    ) -> anyhow::Result<Transition> {\n        match event {\n            NodeEvent::Tick => {\n                info!(\"boot sequence: verifying database connectivity\");\n                ctx.db.healthcheck().await?;\n                info!(\"boot sequence: connecting to peer network\");\n                // Suppose we send some handshake event via ctx.bus here  \n                // ctx.bus.publish(...)\n\n                Ok(Transition::Next(Box::<StateSyncing>::default()))\n            }\n            NodeEvent::Shutdown => Ok(Transition::Shutdown),\n            _ => Ok(Transition::Stay),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Synchronising blockchain data with peers.\n#[derive(Default)]\nstruct StateSyncing;\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl State for StateSyncing {\n    fn name(&self) -> &'static str {\n        \"Syncing\"\n    }\n\n    #[instrument(skip_all)]\n    async fn on_event(\n        &mut self,\n        ctx: &mut NodeContext,\n        event: NodeEvent,\n    ) -> anyhow::Result<Transition> {\n        match event {\n            NodeEvent::BlockReceived(block) => {\n                info!(height = block.header.height, \"received block during sync\");\n                ctx.db.insert_block(block).await?;\n                // For brevity we assume once at tip we move to Active\n                if ctx.db.is_at_chain_tip().await? {\n                    info!(\"local chain at tip \u2013 moving to Active state\");\n                    return Ok(Transition::Next(Box::<StateActive>::default()));\n                }\n                Ok(Transition::Stay)\n            }\n            NodeEvent::Shutdown => Ok(Transition::Shutdown),\n            _ => Ok(Transition::Stay),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Fully synced, participating in consensus and answering RPCs.\n#[derive(Default)]\nstruct StateActive;\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl State for StateActive {\n    fn name(&self) -> &'static str {\n        \"Active\"\n    }\n\n    #[instrument(skip_all)]\n    async fn on_event(\n        &mut self,\n        ctx: &mut NodeContext,\n        event: NodeEvent,\n    ) -> anyhow::Result<Transition> {\n        match event {\n            NodeEvent::ElectedComposer if ctx.config.is_validator => {\n                info!(\"\ud83c\udfb5 This node has been elected composer \u2013 creating art block\");\n                let block = compose_next_block(ctx).await?;\n                ctx.bus.publish(NodeEvent::BlockReceived(block.clone()))\n                    .await\n                    .map_err(|e| anyhow::anyhow!(\"failed to publish block: {e}\"))?;\n                ctx.db.insert_block(block).await?;\n                Ok(Transition::Stay)\n            }\n            NodeEvent::BlockReceived(block) => {\n                debug!(\n                    height = block.header.height,\n                    composer = %block.header.producer,\n                    \"applying canonical block\"\n                );\n                ctx.db.insert_block(block).await?;\n                Ok(Transition::Stay)\n            }\n            NodeEvent::Shutdown => Ok(Transition::Shutdown),\n            _ => Ok(Transition::Stay),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Terminal error state\u2014any failure bubbles here so that the system can exit\n/// gracefully instead of panicking.\n#[derive(Debug)]\nstruct StateError {\n    cause: anyhow::Error,\n}\n\nimpl StateError {\n    fn new<E: Into<anyhow::Error>>(e: E) -> Self {\n        Self { cause: e.into() }\n    }\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl State for StateError {\n    fn name(&self) -> &'static str {\n        \"Error\"\n    }\n\n    async fn on_event(\n        &mut self,\n        _ctx: &mut NodeContext,\n        _event: NodeEvent,\n    ) -> anyhow::Result<Transition> {\n        error!(\"node is in error state: {:?}\", self.cause);\n        Ok(Transition::Shutdown)\n    }\n}\n\n// ------------------------------\n// Helper functions\n// ------------------------------\n\n/// Compose a new \u201cart block\u201d as elected composer.\n///\n/// This is merely a stub for the example.  A real implementation would run the\n/// Proof-of-Inspiration algorithm, gather pending transactions from the mem-\n/// pool, merge generative art layers, compute state roots, sign the header,\n/// etc.\nasync fn compose_next_block(ctx: &NodeContext) -> anyhow::Result<Block> {\n    use rand::Rng;\n\n    let mut rng = rand::thread_rng();\n    let block = Block {\n        header: crate::network::types::BlockHeader {\n            height: ctx.db.latest_height().await? + 1,\n            producer: ctx.config.node_id.clone(),\n            timestamp: chrono::Utc::now(),\n            nonce: rng.gen::<u64>(),\n            prev_hash: ctx.db.latest_hash().await?,\n            merkle_root: vec![0; 32], // placeholder\n            signature: vec![],\n        },\n        transactions: vec![],\n    };\n    Ok(block)\n}\n\n// ------------------------------\n// Tests\n// ------------------------------\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use tokio::time::timeout;\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn test_boot_to_shutdown() {\n        let (tx, rx) = mpsc::channel(8);\n        let cfg = NodeConfig {\n            is_validator: false,\n            ..Default::default()\n        };\n        let _handle = NodeStateMachine::spawn(NodeContext::new(cfg, tx.clone()), rx);\n\n        // Ask the machine to shutdown\n        tx.send(NodeEvent::Shutdown).await.unwrap();\n\n        // Wait a short time to ensure completion\n        // we don't assert on output; test just ensures no panic.\n        timeout(Duration::from_secs(1), async { tokio::task::yield_now().await })\n            .await\n            .unwrap();\n    }\n}\n```",

Factory & Strategy pattern\u2013powered NFT minting logic.\n//! Creates multilayer NFTs, signs mint payloads with a pluggable crypto\n//! backend and broadcasts events onto the internal event-bus.\n//!\n//! This file purposefully hides transport concerns (gRPC, HTTP, etc.); the\n//! factory is a pure domain component that can be wired into whatever\n//! outer-layer the micro-service exposes.\n\nuse pub tx_hash: String,\n    pub signature: Vec<u8>,\n}\n\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n/// Error Handling\n/// {0}\")]\n    InvalidRoyalty(u16),\n    #[error(\"mint payload validation error: {0}\")]\n    Validation(String),\n    #[error(\"crypto error: {0}\")]\n    Crypto(#[from] CryptoError),\n    #[error(\"blockchain client error: {0}\")]\n    Blockchain(#[from] BlockchainError),\n    #[error(\"event bus error: {0}\")]\n    EventBus(#[from] EventBusError),\n}\n\n#[derive(Error, Debug)]\npub
