{\n    #[error(\"node unreachable\")]\n    NodeUnreachable,\n    #[error(\"transaction rejected: {0}\")]\n    TransactionRejected(String),\n}\n\n#[derive(Error, Debug)]\npub enum EventBusError {\n    #[error(\"publish failed\")]\n    PublishFailed,\n}\n\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n/// Traits (Strategy / Port abstractions)\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n/// Unified crypto-signer strategy so we can swap Ed25519, BLS, PQ, etc.\n#[async_trait]\npub trait CryptoSigner: Send + Sync {\n    /// \u2018Human\u2019 name of the algorithm (ed25519, bls12381, falcon, \u2026).\n    fn algorithm(&self) -> &'static str;\n\n    /// Public identifier derived from the secret key (hex / bech32).\n    fn public_key(&self) -> String;\n\n    /// Sign arbitrary message bytes.\n    async fn sign(&self, message: &[u8]) -> Result<Vec<u8>, CryptoError>;\n}\n\n/// Port for whatever chain client we\u2019re using (substrate, cosmos, homework-chain).\n#[async_trait]\npub trait BlockchainClient: Send + Sync {\n    async fn submit_mint(&self, payload: MintPayload) -> Result<String, BlockchainError>;\n    async fn latest_token_id(&self) -> Result<u64, BlockchainError>;\n}\n\n/// Simplistic event bus publisher (fan-out / kafka / nats / anything).\n#[async_trait]\npub trait EventPublisher: Send + Sync {\n    async fn publish<M: Serialize + Send + Sync>(&self, topic: &str, msg: &M) -> Result<(), EventBusError>;\n}\n\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n/// NFT Factory (Concrete implementation of the Factory pattern)\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n/// Shared reference-counted pointer to immutable factory configuration.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct FactoryConfig {\n    /// Maximum allowed royalty (bps). Prevents creator mistakes.\n    pub max_royalty_bps: u16,\n    /// Event bus topic for successful mints.\n    pub event_topic_success: String,\n    /// Event bus topic for failed mints.\n    pub event_topic_failure: String,\n}\n\npub struct NftFactory<S, C, E>\nwhere\n    S: CryptoSigner,\n    C: BlockchainClient,\n    E: EventPublisher,\n{\n    signer: Arc<S>,\n    chain: Arc<C>,\n    bus: Arc<E>,\n    config: Arc<FactoryConfig>,\n    // optionally keep some internal state (metrics, counters, etc.)\n    minted_counter: RwLock<u64>,\n}\n\nimpl<S, C, E> NftFactory<S, C, E>\nwhere\n    S: CryptoSigner + 'static,\n    C: BlockchainClient + 'static,\n    E: EventPublisher + 'static,\n{\n    pub fn new(signer: Arc<S>, chain: Arc<C>, bus: Arc<E>, config: FactoryConfig) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            signer,\n            chain,\n            bus,\n            config: Arc::new(config),\n            minted_counter: RwLock::new(0),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Validate, sign, submit and broadcast the mint request.\n    #[instrument(skip_all, level = \"info\", fields(creator = %req.creator_wallet))]\n    pub async fn mint_nft(&self, req: MintRequest) -> Result<NftReceipt, FactoryError> {\n        self.validate_request(&req)?;\n\n        // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n        // 1. Serialize metadata to JSON; in reality we would push to IPFS/Arweave\n        // and obtain a CID, we\u2019ll fake it by hashing the JSON.\n        // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n        let metadata_json = serde_json::to_vec(&req)\n            .map_err(|e| FactoryError::Validation(format!(\"metadata serialization: {e}\")))?;\n\n        let metadata_cid = hex::encode(blake3::hash(&metadata_json).as_bytes());\n\n        // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n        // 2. Build chain payload and sign it with the selected algorithm.\n        // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n        let idempotency_key = Uuid::new_v4();\n        let mut payload_bytes = Vec::new();\n        payload_bytes.extend_from_slice(idempotency_key.as_bytes());\n        payload_bytes.extend_from_slice(metadata_cid.as_bytes());\n        payload_bytes.extend_from_slice(&req.royalty_bps.to_le_bytes());\n        payload_bytes.extend_from_slice(req.creator_wallet.as_bytes());\n        payload_bytes.extend_from_slice(&req.nonce.to_le_bytes());\n\n        let signature = self.signer.sign(&payload_bytes).await?;\n\n        let payload = MintPayload {\n            idempotency_key,\n            creator_wallet: req.creator_wallet.clone(),\n            metadata_cid,\n            royalty_bps: req.royalty_bps,\n            signature: signature.clone(),\n        };\n\n        // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n        // 3. Submit mint extrinsic / transaction to the chain.\n        // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n        let tx_hash = match self.chain.submit_mint(payload.clone()).await {\n            Ok(h) => h,\n            Err(e) => {\n                // fire & forget failure event\n                let _ = self\n                    .bus\n                    .publish(\n                        &self.config.event_topic_failure,\n                        &MintFailureEvent::from_request(&req, &format!(\"{e}\")),\n                    )\n                    .await;\n                return Err(e.into());\n            }\n        };\n\n        // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n        // 4. Retrieve token ID (optimistic assumption we mint sequentially).\n        // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n        let token_id = self.chain.latest_token_id().await?;\n\n        // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n        // 5. Bump metrics & broadcast success event.\n        // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n        {\n            let mut counter = self.minted_counter.write().await;\n            *counter += 1;\n        }\n\n        let receipt = NftReceipt {\n            token_id,\n            tx_hash: tx_hash.clone(),\n            signature,\n        };\n\n        self.bus\n            .publish(&self.config.event_topic_success, &receipt)\n            .await?;\n\n        info!(token_id, tx_hash, \"NFT minted successfully\");\n        Ok(receipt)\n    }\n\n    // -------------------\n    // internal helpers\n    // -------------------\n    fn validate_request(&self, req: &MintRequest) -> Result<(), FactoryError> {\n        if req.royalty_bps > self.config.max_royalty_bps {\n            return Err(FactoryError::InvalidRoyalty(req.royalty_bps));\n        }\n        if req.layers.is_empty() {\n            return Err(FactoryError::Validation(\"at least one layer required\".into()));\n        }\n        if req.creator_wallet.trim().is_empty() {\n            return Err(FactoryError::Validation(\"creator_wallet is empty\".into()));\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n/// Event Definitions\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize)]\nstruct MintFailureEvent {\n    pub creator_wallet: String,\n    pub timestamp_ms: u128,\n    pub reason: String,\n}\n\nimpl MintFailureEvent {\n    fn from_request(req: &MintRequest, reason: &str) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            creator_wallet: req.creator_wallet.clone(),\n            timestamp_ms: SystemTime::now()\n                .duration_since(UNIX_EPOCH)\n                .expect(\"system time ok\")\n                .as_millis(),\n            reason: reason.to_string(),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n/// Dummy/Mock implementations behind \u2018test\u2019 feature so we can run unit tests.\n/// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use std::sync::Mutex;\n\n    // --------------------\n    // Mock crypto signer\n    // --------------------\n    struct MockSigner;\n    #[async_trait]\n    impl CryptoSigner for MockSigner {\n        fn algorithm(&self) -> &'static str {\n            \"mocked-ed25519\"\n        }\n\n        fn public_key(&self) -> String {\n            \"deadbeef\".to_string()\n        }\n\n        async fn sign(&self, message: &[u8]) -> Result<Vec<u8>, CryptoError> {\n            Ok(blake3::hash(message).as_bytes().to_vec())\n        }\n    }\n\n    // --------------------\n    // Mock chain client\n    // --------------------\n    struct MockChain {\n        counter: Mutex<u64>,\n    }\n\n    #[async_trait]\n    impl BlockchainClient for MockChain {\n        async fn submit_mint(&self, _payload: MintPayload) -> Result<String, BlockchainError> {\n            let mut c = self.counter.lock().unwrap();\n            *c += 1;\n            Ok(format!(\"0x{:x}\", *c))\n        }\n\n        async fn latest_token_id(&self) -> Result<u64, BlockchainError> {\n            let c = self.counter.lock().unwrap();\n            Ok(*c)\n        }\n    }\n\n    // --------------------\n    // Mock event bus\n    // --------------------\n    struct MockBus;\n    #[async_trait]\n    impl EventPublisher for MockBus {\n        async fn publish<M: Serialize + Send + This module is responsible for orchestrating the full life-cycle of NFT\n//! listings in the CanvasChain Symphony marketplace micro-service.  \n//! It follows Repository + Event Driven patterns to keep storage concerns and\n//! side-effects clearly separated from business logic.\n//!\n//! Responsibilities\n//! * Create / update / cancel fixed-price listings\n//! * Atomically settle purchases (reserve \u2192 transfer \u2192 close)\n//! * Publish `MarketplaceEvent`s on the internal event bus\n//! * Provide a type-safe fa\u00e7ade for gRPC handlers & GraphQL resolvers\n//!\n//! Note: In production, `ListingRepository` would be backed by Postgres or\n//! RocksDB; here we ship an in-memory implementation for completeness.\n\n#![allow(clippy::large_enum_variant)]\n\nuse std::{\n    collections::HashMap,\n    sync::Arc,\n    time::Duration,\n};\n\nuse async_trait::async_trait;\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\nuse rust_decimal::Decimal;\nuse tokio::{\n    sync::{broadcast, RwLock},\n    time::timeout,\n};\nuse tracing::{debug, error, info, \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n#[derive(Debug, Hash)]\npub struct AccountId(Uuid);\n\nimpl AccountId {\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self(Uuid::new_v4())\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]\npub enum ListingStatus {\n    Active,\n    Reserved { buyer: AccountId, reserved_at: DateTime<Utc> },\n    Sold,\n    Cancelled,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct Listing {\n    pub id: ListingId,\n    pub owner: ListingStatus::Active => {\n                listing.status = ListingStatus::Reserved {\n                    buyer,\n                    reserved_at: Utc::now(),\n                };\n self.repo.get(listing_id))\n            .await\n            .map_err(|_| ListingError::Timeout)??\n            ;\n\n        if listing.owner != caller {\n            return without reservation\n            }\n            ListingStatus::Reserved { buyer: reserved_buyer, .. } if *reserved_buyer == buyer => {}\n            ListingStatus::Reserved { buyer: reserved_buyer, .. } => {\n                return Err(ListingError::Reserved(*reserved_buyer));\n            }\n            ListingStatus::Sold => return Err(ListingError::AlreadySold),\n            ListingStatus::Cancelled => return Err(ListingError::AlreadyCancelled),\n        }\n\n        // TODO: integrate with payment processor / smart contract to transfer funds & NFT\n\n        // When settlement succeeds:\n        listing.status = ListingStatus::Sold;\n        listing.updated_at = Utc::now();\n\n        timeout(DB_OP_TIMEOUT, self.repo.update(listing.clone()))\n            .await\n            .map_err(|_| ListingError::Timeout)??\n            ;\n\n        self.dispatch_event(MarketplaceEvent::ListingPurchased { listing_id, buyer })?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n .await\n            .map_err(|_| ListingError::Timeout)?\n    }\n\n    #[instrument(skip(self))]\n    pub async fn list_active(&self) -> Result<Vec<Listing>, ListingError> {\n     "content": "```rust\n//! Auction engine for the marketplace micro-service.\n//!\n//! Responsibilities\n//! ----------------\n//! 1. Create, store and track English auctions for multilayer NFTs.\n//! 2. Enforce bidding rules (reserve price, minimum increment, anti-sniping).\n//! 3. Periodically finalize ended auctions and emit events onto the service bus.\n//!\n//! The engine is designed for dependency-injection: any persistent storage that\n//! implements `AuctionStore` can be plugged in.  Out of the box we provide an\n//! in-memory implementation that is perfect for unit tests and local dev\n//! environments.\n//!\n//! The module is *asynchronous* and uses Tokio for non-blocking execution.\n//!\n//! # Example\n//! ```no_run\n//! # use marketplace_service::auction_engine::*;\n//! # #[tokio::main]\n//! # async fn main() -> anyhow::Result<()> {\n//! let engine = AuctionEngine::with_memory_store(Default::default());\n//!\n//! let auction_id = engine\n//!     .create_auction(CreateAuction {\n//!         nft_id: NftId::new(),\n//!         seller_id: UserId::new(),\n//!         reserve_price: 10_000,\n//!         duration: chrono::Duration::hours(24),\n//!     })\n//!     .await?;\n//!\n//! engine\n//!     .place_bid(auction_id, UserId::new(), 11_000)\n//!     .await?;\n//!\n//! // spawn finalize loop\n//! engine.clone().spawn_finalize_loop(tokio::time::Duration::from_secs(30));\n//! # Ok(()) }\n//! ```\n\nuse std::{\n    collections::HashMap,\n    fmt,\n    sync::Arc,\n    time::Duration as StdDuration,\n};\n\nuse async_trait::async_trait;\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Duration, Utc};\nuse -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                                Type Aliases                                */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n#[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Eq, PartialEq, Hash, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct AuctionId(Uuid);\n\nimpl AuctionId {\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self(Uuid::new_v4())\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Eq, PartialEq, Hash, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct UserId(Uuid);\n\nimpl UserId {\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self(Uuid::new_v4())\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Eq, PartialEq, Hash, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct NftId(Uuid);\n\nimpl NftId {\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self(Uuid::new_v4())\n    }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                                 DTOs / API                                 */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/// Immutable auction parameters used for construction.\n#[derive(Debug)]\npub struct CreateAuction {\n    pub nft_id: NftId,\n    pub seller_id: UserId,\n    /// Minimum price in the platform's smallest denomination (e.g. wei).\n    pub reserve_price: u128,\n    /// How long the auction should stay active.\n    pub duration: Duration,\n}\n\n/// Public view of a bid.\n#[derive(Clone, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct Bid {\n    pub bidder_id: UserId,\n    pub amount: u128,\n    pub timestamp: DateTime<Utc>,\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                                  Domain                                    */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n#[derive(Clone, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum AuctionStatus {\n    Pending,\n    Active,\n    Finalized,\n    Cancelled,\n}\n\n#[derive(Clone, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct Auction {\n    pub id: AuctionId,\n    pub nft_id: NftId,\n    pub seller_id: UserId,\n    pub reserve_price: u128,\n    pub start_time: DateTime<Utc>,\n    pub end_time: DateTime<Utc>,\n    pub status: AuctionStatus,\n    pub highest_bid: Option<Bid>,\n}\n\nimpl Auction {\n    /// Returns whether the auction is open for bids.\n    pub fn is_active(&self, now: DateTime<Utc>) -> bool {\n        matches!(self.status, AuctionStatus::Active)\n            && now >= self.start_time\n            && now < self.end_time\n    }\n\n    /// Returns whether auction should be finalized (elapsed or cancelled).\n    pub fn should_finalize(&self, now: DateTime<Utc>) -> bool {\n        matches!(self.status, AuctionStatus::Active) && now >= self.end_time\n    }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                                    Store                                   */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/// Storage abstraction. Can be backed by Postgres, Redis, RocksDB, etc.\n#[async_trait]\npub trait AuctionStore: Send + Sync + 'static {\n    async fn insert(&self, auction: Auction) -> Result<(), EngineError>;\n    async fn update(&self, auction: &Auction) -> Result<(), EngineError>;\n    async fn get(&self, id: AuctionId) -> Result<Option<Auction>, EngineError>;\n    async fn all_due_for_finalize(\n        &self,\n        now: DateTime<Utc>,\n    ) -> Result<Vec<AuctionId>, EngineError>;\n}\n\n/* --------------------------- In-memory implementation --------------------------- */\n\ntype AuctionMap = Arc<RwLock<HashMap<AuctionId, Auction>>>;\n\n/// An in-memory, thread-safe store backed by a `HashMap`.\n/// Meant for tests / local development, *not* production.\n#[derive(Clone, Default)]\npub struct MemoryAuctionStore {\n    map: AuctionMap,\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl AuctionStore for MemoryAuctionStore {\n    async fn insert(&self, auction: Auction) -> Result<(), EngineError> {\n        let mut map = self.map.write().await;\n        map.insert(auction.id, auction);\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    async fn update(&self, auction: &Auction) -> Result<(), EngineError> {\n        let mut map = self.map.write().await;\n        if let Some(a) = map.get_mut(&auction.id) {\n            *a = auction.clone();\n            Ok(())\n        } else {\n            Err(EngineError::AuctionNotFound)\n        }\n    }\n\n    async fn get(&self, id: AuctionId) -> Result<Option<Auction>, EngineError> {\n        let map = self.map.read().await;\n        Ok(map.get(&id).cloned())\n    }\n\n    async fn all_due_for_finalize(\n        &self,\n        now: DateTime<Utc>,\n    ) -> Result<Vec<AuctionId>, EngineError> {\n        let map = self.map.read().await;\n        Ok(map\n            .values()\n            .filter(|a| a.should_finalize(now))\n            .map(|a| a.id)\n            .collect())\n    }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                               Event definitions                            */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n#[derive(Clone, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum AuctionEvent {\n    AuctionCreated(AuctionId),\n    BidPlaced Option<u128>,\n    },\n    AuctionCancelled(AuctionId),\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                               Error handling                               */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum EngineError {\n    #[error(\"auction not found\")]\n    AuctionNotFound,\n    #[error(\"auction is not active\")]\n    AuctionNotActive,\n    #[error(\"bid below reserve price\")]\n    ReserveNotMet,\n    #[error(\"bid increment too low\")]\n    IncrementTooLow,\n    #[error(\"seller cannot bid on own auction\")]\n    SellerCannotBid,\n    #[error(\"auction already finalized or cancelled\")]\n    InvalidAuctionState,\n    #[error(\"storage error: {0}\")]\n    Storage(#[from] anyhow::Error),\n    #[error(\"broadcast error\")]\n    Broadcast,\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                                AuctionEngine                               */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct AuctionEngine<S: AuctionStore> {\n    store: Arc<S>,\n    /// Minimum bid increment (e.g. 1% of current highest) expressed as basis points.\n    min_increment_bps: u16,\n    /// Tokio broadcast channel for events.\n    event_tx: broadcast::Sender<AuctionEvent>,\n}\n\nimpl<S: AuctionStore> AuctionEngine<S> {\n    /// Create an engine using the provided store.\n    pub fn new(store: S, min_increment_bps: u16) -> Self {\n        let (event_tx, _) = broadcast::channel(1024);\n        Self {\n            store: Arc::new(store),\n            min_increment_bps,\n            event_tx,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Convenience helper for tests/local dev.\n    pub fn with_memory_store(config: EngineConfig) -> Self {\n        Self::new(MemoryAuctionStore::default(), config.min_increment_bps)\n    }\n\n    /// Subscribe to auction events (fire-and-forget).\n    pub fn subscribe(&self) -> broadcast::Receiver<AuctionEvent> {\n        self.event_tx.subscribe()\n    }\n\n    /* ----------------------------- API methods ----------------------------- */\n\n    /// Creates an auction and stores it. Emits `AuctionCreated`.\n    pub async fn create_auction(\n        &self,\n        params: CreateAuction,\n    ) -> Result<AuctionId, EngineError> {\n        let now = Utc::now();\n        let auction = Auction {\n            id: AuctionId::new(),\n            nft_id: params.nft_id,\n            seller_id: params.seller_id,\n            reserve_price: params.reserve_price,\n            start_time: now,\n            end_time: now + params.duration,\n            status: AuctionStatus::Active,\n            highest_bid: None,\n        };\n        self.store.insert(auction.clone()).await?;\n        self.emit(AuctionEvent::AuctionCreated(auction.id))?;\n        Ok(auction.id)\n    }\n\n    /// Places a new bid on an active auction.\n    pub async fn place_bid(\n        &self,\n        auction_id: AuctionId,\n        bidder_id: UserId,\n        amount: u128,\n    ) -> Result<(), EngineError> {\n        let now = Utc::now();\n        let mut auction = match self.store.get(auction_id).await? {\n            Some(a) => a,\n            None => return Err(EngineError::AuctionNotFound),\n        };\n\n        if !auction.is_active(now) {\n            return Err(EngineError::AuctionNotActive);\n        }\n\n        if bidder_id == auction.seller_id {\n            return Err(EngineError::SellerCannotBid);\n        }\n\n        // First bid must be >= reserve.\n        if auction.highest_bid.is_none() && amount < auction.reserve_price {\n            return Err(EngineError::ReserveNotMet);\n        }\n\n        // Ensure minimum increment.\n        if let Some(ref high) = auction.highest_bid {\n            let min_required =\n                high.amount + Self::calc_increment(high.amount, self.min_increment_bps);\n            if amount < min_required {\n                return Err(EngineError::IncrementTooLow);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // TODO: anti-sniping extension window can be applied here.\n\n        auction.highest_bid = Some(Bid {\n            bidder_id,\n            amount,\n            timestamp: now,\n        });\n\n        self.store.update(&auction).await?;\n        self.emit(AuctionEvent::BidPlaced {\n            auction_id,\n            bidder_id,\n            amount,\n        })?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Cancels an auction by its seller before any bids are placed.\n    pub async fn cancel_auction(\n        &self,\n        auction_id: AuctionId,\n        requester: UserId,\n    ) -> Result<(), EngineError> {\n        let mut auction = match self.store.get(auction_id).await? {\n            Some(a) => a,\n            None => return Err(EngineError::AuctionNotFound),\n        };\n\n        if auction.seller_id != requester {\n            return Err(EngineError::InvalidAuctionState);\n        }\n\n        if auction.highest_bid.is_some() || !matches!(auction.status, AuctionStatus::Active) {\n            return Err(EngineError::InvalidAuctionState);\n        }\n\n        auction.status = AuctionStatus::Cancelled;\n        self.store.update(&auction).await?;\n        self.emit(AuctionEvent::AuctionCancelled(auction_id))?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Finalize an auction that reached its end time. Returns the winner if any.\n    pub async fn finalize_auction(\n        &self,\n        auction_id: AuctionId,\n    ) -> Result<Option<(UserId, u128)>, EngineError> {\n        let mut auction = match self.store.get(auction_id).await? {\n            Some(a) => a,\n            None => return Err(EngineError::AuctionNotFound),\n        };\n\n        if !auction.should_finalize(Utc::now()) {\n            return Err(EngineError::InvalidAuctionState);\n        }\n\n        auction.status = AuctionStatus::Finalized;\n        let winner_info = auction\n            .highest_bid\n            .as_ref()\n            .map(|b| (b.bidder_id, b.amount));\n\n        self.store.update(&auction).await?;\n        self.emit(AuctionEvent::AuctionFinalized {\n            auction_id,\n            winner: winner_info.map(|t| t.0),\n            amount: winner_info.map(|t| t.1),\n        })?;\n\n        // TODO: trigger settlement workflow (escrow smart contract, royalties, etc.)\n        Ok(winner_info)\n    }\n\n    /* ------------------------------- Internals ------------------------------ */\n\n    fn emit(&self, evt: AuctionEvent) -> Result<(), EngineError> {\n        self.event_tx\n            .send(evt)\n            .map_err(|_| EngineError::Broadcast)\n            .map(|_| ())\n    }\n\n    fn calc_increment(current: u128, bps: u16) -> u128 {\n        // basis points: 1 bps = 0.01 %\n        (current * bps as u128) / 10_000u128\n    }\n\n    /* ----------------------------- Finalize loop ---------------------------- */\n\n    /// Spawns a Tokio task that periodically finalizes elapsed auctions.\n    ///\n    /// NOTE: In a clustered deployment only the leader instance should run the\n    /// loop to avoid double-finalization.  This is achieved via distributed\n    /// locks (e.g. etcd/consul) at the service orchestrator layer.\n    pub fn spawn_finalize_loop(self, interval: StdDuration) -> JoinHandle<()> {\n        tokio::spawn(async move {\n            let mut ticker = tokio::time::interval(interval);\n            loop {\n                ticker.tick().await;\n                let now = Utc::now();\n                match self.store.all_due_for_finalize(now).await {\n                    Ok(ids) => {\n                        for id in ids {\n                            // best effort, log errors\n                            if let Err(e) = self.finalize_auction(id).await {\n                                tracing::warn!(\n                                    auction_id = ?id,\n                                    error = ?e,\n                                    \"failed to finalize auction\"\n                                );\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                    Err(e) => tracing::error!(error = ?e, \"finalize loop failed to fetch auctions\"),\n                }\n            }\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                              Engine configuration                          */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct EngineConfig {\n    pub min_increment_bps: u16,\n}\n\nimpl Default for EngineConfig {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self { min_increment_bps: 50 } // 0.5%\n    }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                                   Display                                  */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nimpl fmt::Display for AuctionId {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n        self.0.fmt(f)\n    }\n}\n```",

The module follows a Strategy pattern where each curve implements the\n//! `SigningCurve` trait. \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n/// self\n            .curves\n            .get(algo)\n            .ok_or(KeyManagerError::UnsupportedAlgorithm)?;\n\n        // 1) Generate a fresh keypair\n        let (sk, pk) = curve.generate()?;\n\n        // 2) Encrypt the secret key with Argon2 + ChaCha20-Poly1305\n        let (ciphertext, salt, nonce) = encrypt_secret(password, &sk)?;\n\n        // 3) Store on disk\n        let wallet = KeyManagerError> {\n        let meta = self\n            .keystore\n            .get(id)\n            .await?\n            .ok_or(KeyManagerError::WalletNotFound)?;\n\n        let curve = self\n            .curves\n            .get(meta.algo)\n            .ok_or(KeyManagerError::UnsupportedAlgorithm)?;\n\n        let sk = decrypt_secret(\n            password,\n            &meta.encrypted_sk,\n Signing curves (Strategy pattern)\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n/// Strategy trait for crypto curves.\npub trait SigningCurve: Send + Sync {\n    fn algorithm(&self) -> CryptoAlgorithm;\n\n    /// Generate a fresh keypair.\n    fn generate(&self) -> Result<(Vec<u8>, \u2013 primarily for unit tests.\n    #[allow(dead_code)]\n    fn verify(\n        &self,\n        public: &[u8],\n        message: &[u8],\n        signature: &[u8],\n    ) -> Result<(), KeyManagerError>;\n}\n\n/// Registry holding all curve implementations.\n#[derive(Default, Clone)]\nstruct CurveRegistry {\n    curves: Arc<RwLock<Vec<Box<dyn SigningCurve>>>>,\n}\n\nimpl CurveRegistry {\n    fn register(&mut self, curve: Box<dyn SigningCurve>) {\n        tokio::task::block_in_place(|| {\n            let mut guard = futures::executor::block_on(self.curves.write());\n            guard.push(curve);\n        });\n    }\n\n    fn get(&self, algo: CryptoAlgorithm) -> Option<&dyn SigningCurve> {\n        tokio::task::block_in_place(|| {\n            let guard = futures::executor::block_on(self.curves.read());\n            guard\n                .iter()\n                .find(|c| c.algorithm() == algo)\n                .map(|b| b.as_ref())\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 Ed25519 Symphony services (or external clients) create wallets, query balances,\n//! transfer tokens and sign arbitrary messages.  \n//!\n//! Internally the server is backed by a pluggable [`WalletBackend`] trait.\n//! The default backend (`SledBackend`) stores encrypted key-material in a\n//! Sled embedded database and uses ed25519\u2010dalek for signing.  Backends can\n//! be swapped at runtime (Strategy pattern) which makes it trivial to\n//! upgrade to BLS, post-quantum or hardware-based signing in the future.\n//!\n//! # Conventions\n//!\n//! * All monetary amounts are expressed in **atomic units** (u128).\n//! * Hex-encoded strings are expected to be lowercase, without `0x` prefix.\n//! * Errors are mapped to gRPC `Status` codes using a custom [`WalletError`]\n//!   \u2192 [`tonic::Status`] conversion.\n\n#![allow(clippy::missing_errors_doc)]\n#![allow(clippy::missing_panics_doc)]\n\nuse std::{net::SocketAddr, path::PathBuf, sync::Arc};\n\nuse async_trait::async_trait;\nuse ed25519_dalek::{Keypair, PublicKey, Signature, Signer, PUBLIC_KEY_LENGTH};\nuse rand::rngs::OsRng;\nuse thiserror::Error;\nuse tokio::sync::RwLock;\nuse tonic::{transport::Server, Request, Response, Status};\nuse tracing::{error, info};\n\nuse crate::config::WalletConfig;\n\n// === Generated code from `protoc` lives in `crate::proto` === //\nuse crate::proto::wallet::{\n    wallet_service_server::{WalletService, WalletServiceServer},\n    BalanceRequest, BalanceResponse, CreateWalletRequest, CreateWalletResponse,\n    SignRequest, SignResponse, TransferRequest, TransferResponse,\n};\n\n// =========================================================================\n//  Domain errors\n// =========================================================================\n\n/// All domain-level errors produced by the wallet service.\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum WalletError {\n    #[error(\"wallet `{0}` not found\")]\n    WalletNotFound(String),\n\n    #[error(\"insufficient funds (available: {available}, required: {required})\")]\n    InsufficientFunds { available: u128, required: u128 },\n\n    #[error(\"database error: {0}\")]\n    Db(#[from] sled::Error),\n\n    #[error(\"signature failure: {0}\")]\n    Signature(String),\n\n    #[error(\"unsupported cryptographic backend\")]\n    UnsupportedBackend,\n\n    #[error(\"internal error: {0}\")]\n    Internal(String),\n}\n\nimpl From<WalletError> for Status {\n    fn from(err: WalletError) -> Self {\n        match err {\n            WalletError::WalletNotFound(_) => Status::not_found(err.to_string()),\n            WalletError::InsufficientFunds { .. } => Status::failed_precondition(err.to_string()),\n            WalletError::Db(_) | WalletError::Internal(_) => Status::internal(err.to_string()),\n            WalletError::Signature(_) => Status::internal(err.to_string()),\n            WalletError::UnsupportedBackend => Status::unimplemented(err.to_string()),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// =========================================================================\n//  Wallet backend operations.\n#[async_trait]\npub trait WalletBackend: Send + Sync + 'static {\n    async fn create_wallet(&self) -> Result<(String, PublicKey), WalletError>;\n\n    async fn balance(&self, wallet_id:       &self,\n        wallet_id: &str,\n        message: &[u8],\n    ) -> Result<Signature, WalletError>;\n}\n\n// =========================================================================\n// }\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl WalletBackend for SledBackend {\n    async fn create_wallet(&self) -> Result<(String, PublicKey), WalletError> {\n        // Generate new keypair\n        let mut csprng = OsRng {};\n        let keypair = Keypair::generate(&mut csprng);\n        let wallet_id = hex::encode(&keypair.public.to_bytes());\n\n        let record = WalletRecord {\n            keypair,\n            balance: 0u128,\n        };\n        // Serialize\n        let payload = bincode::serialize(&record)\n            .map_err(|e| WalletError::Internal(format!(\"bincode: {e}\")))?;\n\n        self.keys_tree\n            .insert(Self::_wallet_key(&wallet_id), payload)?;\n        self.ledger_tree.insert(wallet_id.as_bytes(), 0u128.to_be_bytes())?;\n        self.db.flush()?;\n\n        Ok((wallet_id, record.keypair.public))\n    }\n\n    async fn balance(&self, wallet_id: &str) -> Result<u128, WalletError> {\n        let raw = self\n            .ledger_tree\n            .get(wallet_id.as_bytes())?\n            .ok_or_else(|| WalletError::WalletNotFound(wallet_id.to_string()))?;\n        let mut bytes = [0u8; 16];\n        bytes.copy_from_slice(&raw);\n        Ok(u128::from_be_bytes(bytes))\n    }\n\n    async fn transfer(\n        &self,\n        from: &str,\n        to: &str,\n        amount: u128,\n    ) -> Result<(), WalletError> {\n        // Sled does not support multi-key transactions; we pessimistically lock the DB.\n        let _guard = self.db.transaction(|db| {\n            let from_balance = {\n                let raw = self\n                    .ledger_tree\n                    .get(from.as_bytes())?\n                    .ok_or(sled::transaction::ConflictableTransactionError::Abort(\n                        WalletError::WalletNotFound(from.into()),\n                    ))?;\n                let mut b = [0u8; 16];\n                b.copy_from_slice(&raw);\n                Ok(u128::from_be_bytes(b))\n            }?;\n\n            if from_balance < amount {\n                return Err(sled::transaction::ConflictableTransactionError::Abort(\n                    WalletError::InsufficientFunds {\n                        available: from_balance,\n                        required: amount,\n                    },\n                ));\n            }\n\n            let to_balance = {\n                let raw =\n                    self.ledger_tree.get(to.as_bytes())?.unwrap_or_else(|| {\n                        // Auto-create destination account\n                        self.ledger_tree.insert(to.as_bytes(), 0u128.to_be_bytes()).unwrap();\n                        sled::IVec::from(&0u128.to_be_bytes()[..])\n                    });\n                let mut b = [0u8; 16];\n                b.copy_from_slice(&raw);\n                u128::from_be_bytes(b)\n            };\n\n            let new_from = (from_balance - amount).to_be_bytes();\n            let new_to = (to_balance + amount).to_be_bytes();\n\n            self.ledger_tree.insert(from.as_bytes(), new_from)?;\n            self.ledger_tree.insert(to.as_bytes(), new_to)?;\n            Ok(())\n        });\n\n        match _guard {\n            Ok(_) => Ok(()),\n            Err(sled::transaction::TransactionError::Abort(e)) => Err(e),\n            Err(e) => Err(WalletError::Db(e.into())),\n        }\n    }\n\n    async fn sign(\n        &self,\n        wallet_id: &str,\n        message: &[u8],\n    ) -> Result<Signature, WalletError> {\n        let raw = self\n            .keys_tree\n            .get(Self::_wallet_key(wallet_id))?\n            .ok_or_else(|| WalletError::WalletNotFound(wallet_id.to_owned()))?;\n        let record: WalletRecord =\n            bincode::deserialize(&raw).map_err(|e| WalletError::Internal(e.to_string()))?;\n        Ok(record.keypair.sign(message))\n    }\n}\n\n//     public_key: hex::encode(public_key.to_bytes()),\n        };\n        Ok(Response::new(resp))\n    }\n\n    async fn balance(\n        &self,\n        req: Request<BalanceRequest>,\n    ) -> Ok(Response::new(BalanceResponse { balance }))\n    }\n\n    async fn transfer(\n        &self,\n        req: Request<TransferRequest>,\n    ) -> Result<Response<TransferResponse>, Status> {\n .add_service(WalletServiceServer::new(server))\n        // Add built-in gRPC health service so Kubernetes liveness probes work.\n        .serve(addr)\n        .await?;\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n```\n",

self.proposals\n            .read()\n            .await\n            .get(&id)\n            .cloned()\n            .ok_or(ProposalError::NotFound(id))\n    }\n\n    async fn save_vote(\n        &self,\n        proposal_id: Uuid,\n        voter: &str,\n        choice: VoteChoice,\n    ) -> Result<(), ProposalError> {\n        let mut map = self.proposals.write().await;\n        let proposal = The caller is responsible for\n    /// signing the payload.\n    ///\n    /// `signature` must verify against `author` and the payload bytes\n    /// (as canonical JSON).\n    pub async fn create_proposal(\n        &self,\n        author: &str,\n        payload: serde_json::Value,\n        signature: &[u8],\n    ) -> Result<Uuid, ProposalError> {\n        let json_bytes = {\n                proposal_id: proposal.id,\n                author: author.to_owned(),\n            })\n            .await;\n\n        Ok(proposal.id)\n    }\n\n    /// Cast a vote on an active &msg, signature).await?;\n\n        self.store\n            .save_vote(proposal_id, voter, choice)\n            .await\n            .map_err(|e| {\n                debug!(\"save_vote failed: {e}\");\n                e\n            })?;\n\n        self.events\n            .publish(GovernanceEvent::VoteCast {\n                proposal_id,\n                voter: voter.to_owned(),\n                choice,\n            })\n            .await;\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Forces finalization of an active proposal, ignoring `expires_at`\n    /// (useful for emergency admin operations).\n    pub async fn finalize_now(&self, proposal_id: Uuid) -> Result<(), ProposalError> {\n        let proposal = self.store.load_proposal(proposal_id).await?;\n        let outcome = compute_outcome(&proposal, &self.config);\n        self.store.finalize(proposal_id, outcome).await?;\n        self.events\n            .publish(GovernanceEvent::ProposalFinalized { proposal_id, result: outcome })\n            .await;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n/// Computes the outcome according to yes/no/abstain counts and the\n/// engine\u2019s governance parameters.\nfn compute_outcome(proposal: &Proposal, params: &GovernanceParameters) -> ProposalOutcome {\n    let total_votes = proposal.votes.len() as u64;\n    if total_votes == 0 {\n        return ProposalOutcome::QuorumNotMet;\n    }\n\n    let yes = proposal\n        .votes\n        .values()\n        .filter(|&&c| c == VoteChoice::Yes)\n        .count() as u64;\n    let no = proposal\n        .votes\n        .values()\n        .filter(|&&c| c == VoteChoice::No)\n        .count() as u64;\n    let abstain = total_votes - yes - no;\n\n    debug!(\n        \"Computing outcome \u2013 yes:{yes}, no:{no}, abstain:{abstain}, total:{total_votes}\"\n    );\n\n    let quorum_met = (total_votes * 100 / u64::MAX.max(total_votes)) >= params.quorum_pct as u64;\n\n    if !quorum_met {\n        return ProposalOutcome::QuorumNotMet;\n    }\n\n    let yes_pct = yes * 100 / total_votes;\n    if yes_pct >= params.pass_threshold_pct as u64 {\n        ProposalOutcome::Accepted\n    } else {\n        ProposalOutcome::Rejected\n    }\n}\n\n/// Periodic task for auto-finalizing expired proposals.\nasync fn finalize_expired<S: ProposalStore, E: EventPublisher>(\n    store: &Arc<S>,\n    events: &Arc<E>,\n    params: &GovernanceParameters,\n) -> Result<(), ProposalError> {\n    let now = Utc::now();\n    for mut proposal in store.list_active().await? {\n        if proposal.expires_at <= now .publish(GovernanceEvent::ProposalFinalized {\n                    proposal_id: proposal.id,\n                    result: outcome,\n                })\n                .await;\n            info!(\"proposal {} finalized with result {:?}\", proposal.id, outcome);\n        }\n    }\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// A mock signature verifier that accepts 1% of the messages randomly\n/// as invalid.  Replace with a real crypto verifier in production.\npub struct PseudoVerifier;\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl SignatureVerifier for PseudoVerifier {\n    async fn verify(\n        &self,\n        _wallet_address: &str,\n        _payload: &[u8],\n        _signature: &[u8],\n    ) -> Result<(), ProposalError> {\n        let mut rng = rand::thread_rng();\n        let rejected: bool = rng.gen_bool(0.01);\n        if rejected {\n            Err(ProposalError::InvalidSignature)\n        } else {\n            Ok(())\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use serde_json::json;\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn happy_path() {\n        let engine = ProposalEngine::new(\n            Arc::new(InMemoryStore::default()),\n            Arc::new(NullPublisher),\n            Arc::new(PseudoVerifier),\n        );\n\n        let payload = json!({\n            \"type\": \"change_quorum\",\n            \"new_quorum\": 20\n        });\n        let author = \"wallet_1\";\n\n        let proposal_id = engine\n            .create_proposal(author, payload, &[0u8; 64])\n            .await\n            .expect(\"create proposal\");\n\n        engine\n            .cast_vote(proposal_id, \"voter_a\", VoteChoice::Yes, &[0u8; 64])\n            .await\n            .expect(\"vote a\");\n\n        engine\n            .cast_vote(proposal_id, \"voter_b\", VoteChoice::Yes, &[0u8; 64])\n            .await\n            .expect(\"vote b\");\n\n        engine.finalize_now(proposal_id).await.expect(\"finalize\");\n\n        let proposal = engine\n            .store\n            .load_proposal(proposal_id)\n            .await\n            .expect(\"load final\");\n        assert_eq!(proposal.status, ProposalStatus::Finalized);\n    }\n}\n```",

    "content": "```rust\n//! staking_logic.rs\n//!\n//! Core staking & composer\u2013selection logic for the CanvasChain Symphony\n//! staking micro-service.  This file purposefully contains no gRPC or HTTP\n//! plumbing;  it is meant to be embedded by the service\u2010layer binary and\n//! driven by the surrounding transport / storage adapters.\n//!\n//! Architectural notes\n//! -------------------\n//! \u2022 State is kept in-memory behind a `RwLock` and checkpointed by the\n//!   service into persistent storage (e.g. Postgres, RocksDB) \u2013 that part is\n//!   out-of-scope here.\n//! \u2022 Composer selection follows a simplified Proof-of-Inspiration algorithm:\n//!      1. Each staker submits a *VRF proof* for a given round\u2010seed.\n//!      2. The hash output is mapped to `[0, 1)`.  The staker wins if\n//!         output / stake_total < staker_weight.\n//!      3. Ties are broken deterministically by lowest hash.\n//! \u2022 A Strategy pattern exposes pluggable `VrfProvider`s so that collectives\n//!   can experiment with different curves (Ed25519, BLS, PQ, \u2026) without\n//!   recompilation of the other micro-services.\n\nuse std::{\n    collections::HashMap,\n    sync::Arc,\n    time::{Duration, SystemTime},\n};\n\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\nuse rand::{rngs::OsRng, RngCore};\nuse sha2::{Digest, Sha256};\nuse tokio::{\n    sync::{broadcast, RwLock},\n    time,\n};\n\nuse thiserror::Error;\n\n/// Unique user/staker identifier (e.g. wallet address).\npub type StakerId = String;\n/// Result shorthand used throughout the stake logic.\npub type Result<T> = std::result::Result<T, StakingError>;\n\n/// Public event types that can be subscribed to by other micro-services\n/// through the event-bus (`broadcast::Sender`).\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub enum StakingEvent {\n    StakeAdded {\n        staker: StakerId,\n        amount: u128,\n        new_total: u128,\n    },\n    StakeWithdrawn {\n        staker: StakerId,\n        amount: u128,\n        new_total: u128,\n    },\n    ComposerSelected {\n        round: u64,\n        staker: StakerId,\n    },\n}\n\n/// Domain errors emitted by staking logic.\n#[derive(Error, Debug)]\npub enum StakingError {\n    #[error(\"insufficient stake: requested {requested}, available {available}\")]\n    InsufficientStake { requested: u128, available: u128 },\n    #[error(\"staker `{0}` is not registered\")]\n    UnknownStaker(StakerId),\n    #[error(\"VRF verification failed: {0}\")]\n    VrfFailed(String),\n    #[error(\"no stakers registered\")]\n    EmptyPool,\n    #[error(\"attempted to withdraw zero tokens\")]\n    ZeroWithdrawal,\n}\n\n/// Represents an individual staking participant.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct Staker {\n    pub id: StakerId,\n    pub stake: u128,\n    pub last_active: DateTime<Utc>,\n    pub vrf_pubkey: Vec<u8>, // curve is provider specific\n}\n\nimpl Staker {\n    fn new(id: StakerId, initial: u128, vrf_pubkey: Vec<u8>) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            id,\n            stake: initial,\n            last_active: Utc::now(),\n            vrf_pubkey,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Abstraction for a Verifiable Random Function provider.\npub trait VrfProvider: Send + Sync + 'static {\n    /// Produces a VRF proof and output hash for `message` using the *private*\n    /// part of the provider implementation.\n    fn prove(&self, message: &[u8]) -> (Vec<u8> /*proof*/, Vec<u8> /*hash*/);\n\n    /// Verify a proof & hash produced by `prove`.\n    fn verify(\n        &self,\n        public_key: &[u8],\n        message: &[u8],\n        proof: &[u8],\n        hash: &[u8],\n    ) -> std::result::Result<(), String>;\n}\n\n/// Fallback VRF provider that is *not* secure; meant only for local-dev and\n/// CI where cryptography isn\u2019t the focus.  It deterministically hashes the\n/// message + static `private_key`.\npub struct Sha256Vrf {\n    private_key: Vec<u8>,\n}\n\nimpl Sha256Vrf {\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        let mut pk = vec![0u8; 32];\n        OsRng.fill_bytes(&mut pk);\n        Self { private_key: pk }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl VrfProvider for Sha256Vrf {\n    fn prove(&self, message: &[u8]) -> (Vec<u8>, Vec<u8>) {\n        let mut hasher = Sha256::new();\n        hasher.update(&self.private_key);\n        hasher.update(message);\n        let hash = hasher.finalize().to_vec();\n        // `proof` is meaningless here \u2011 we return the key for \u201cverification\u201d\n        (self.private_key.clone(), hash)\n    }\n\n    fn verify(\n        &self,\n        public_key: &[u8],\n        message: &[u8],\n        proof: &[u8],\n        hash: &[u8],\n    ) -> std::result::Result<(), String> {\n        if public_key != proof {\n            return Err(\"public key mismatch\".into());\n        }\n        let mut hasher = Sha256::new();\n        hasher.update(proof); // same as private_key in this dummy impl\n        hasher.update(message);\n        let expected = hasher.finalize();\n        if expected.as_slice() == hash {\n            Ok(())\n        } else {\n            Err(\"hash mismatch\".into())\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Shared staking state guarded by `RwLock`.\n#[derive(Default)]\nstruct StakePoolInner {\n    stakers: HashMap<StakerId, Staker>,\n    total_stake: u128,\n    current_round: u64,\n}\n\n/// Public handle for performing staking operations + composer selection.\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct StakePool {\n    inner: Arc<RwLock<StakePoolInner>>,\n    vrf: Arc<dyn VrfProvider>,\n    event_tx: broadcast::Sender<StakingEvent>,\n}\n\nimpl StakePool {\n    /// Create a new [`StakePool`] with the provided `VrfProvider`.\n    pub fn new(vrf: Arc<dyn VrfProvider>) -> Self {\n        let (event_tx, _) = broadcast::channel(256);\n        Self {\n            inner: Arc::default(),\n            vrf,\n            event_tx,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Subscribe to [`StakingEvent`]s.\n    pub fn subscribe(&self) -> broadcast::Receiver<StakingEvent> {\n        self.event_tx.subscribe()\n    }\n\n    /// Register a new staker or top-up their existing stake.\n    pub async fn add_stake(\n        &self,\n        staker_id: StakerId,\n        vrf_pubkey: Vec<u8>,\n        amount: u128,\n    ) -> Result<()> {\n        let mut inner = self.inner.write().await;\n\n        let entry = inner.stakers.entry(staker_id.clone()).or_insert_with(|| {\n            Staker::new(staker_id.clone(), 0, vrf_pubkey.clone())\n        });\n\n        entry.stake = entry.stake.saturating_add(amount);\n        entry.last_active = Utc::now();\n        inner.total_stake = inner.total_stake.saturating_add(amount);\n\n        self.event_tx.send(StakingEvent::StakeAdded {\n            staker: staker_id,\n            amount,\n            new_total: entry.stake,\n        }).ok();\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Withdraw stake.  Fails if the caller tries to withdraw more than they have.\n    pub async fn withdraw_stake(&self, staker_id: &str, amount: u128) -> Result<()> {\n        if amount == 0 {\n            return Err(StakingError::ZeroWithdrawal);\n        }\n\n        let mut inner = self.inner.write().await;\n        let staker = inner\n            .stakers\n            .get_mut(staker_id)\n            .ok_or_else(|| StakingError::UnknownStaker(staker_id.into()))?;\n\n        if staker.stake < amount {\n            return Err(StakingError::InsufficientStake {\n                requested: amount,\n                available: staker.stake,\n            });\n        }\n\n        staker.stake -= amount;\n        staker.last_active = Utc::now();\n        inner.total_stake -= amount;\n\n        self.event_tx.send(StakingEvent::StakeWithdrawn {\n            staker: staker_id.into(),\n            amount,\n            new_total: staker.stake,\n        }).ok();\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Internal helper to draw a random seed for the next composer round.\n    fn next_round_seed() -> [u8; 32] {\n        let mut seed = [0u8; 32];\n        OsRng.fill_bytes(&mut seed);\n        seed\n    }\n\n    /// Schedule automatic composer selection every `interval`.\n    pub async fn run_composer_election(self: Arc<Self>, interval: Duration) {\n        let mut ticker = time::interval(interval);\n\n        loop {\n            ticker.tick().await;\n            let seed = Self::next_round_seed();\n            match self.select_composer(seed).await {\n                Ok(Some(winner)) => {\n                    tracing::info!(round = self.current_round().await, %winner, \"composer selected\");\n                }\n                Ok(None) => {\n                    // pool is empty\n                }\n                Err(e) => tracing::error!(\"failed to select composer: {e}\"),\n            };\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Return current round number without locking write.\n    pub async fn current_round(&self) -> u64 {\n        self.inner.read().await.current_round\n    }\n\n    /// Execute a single composer election round with the provided seed.\n    /// Returns `Ok(Some(staker_id))` on success, `Ok(None)` if pool empty.\n    /// State changes (round increment) are committed atomically.\n    pub async fn select_composer(&self, seed: [u8; 32]) -> Result<Option<StakerId>> {\n        let mut inner = self.inner.write().await;\n\n        if inner.stakers.is_empty() {\n            return Ok(None);\n        }\n\n        let message = seed; // serialized seed acts as VRF message\n        let mut best_candidate: Option<(StakerId, Vec<u8>)> = None;\n\n        for staker in inner.stakers.values() {\n            // Build domain-separated message: seed || staker-id\n            let mut msg_vec = message.to_vec();\n            msg_vec.extend(staker.id.as_bytes());\n\n            // Each candidate derives a VRF output (hash) \u2013 prove/verify may\n            // happen off-chain in a real system; we shortcut here.\n            let (_proof, hash) = self.vrf.prove(&msg_vec);\n\n            // Map first 16 bytes \u2192 u128 for uniform comparison\n            let mut buf = [0u8; 16];\n            buf.copy_from_slice(&hash[..16]);\n            let rnd = u128::from_be_bytes(buf);\n\n            // Calculate target: (rnd / 2^128) < (stake / total)\n            // Reorder: rnd * total < stake * 2^128\n            let left = rnd.saturating_mul(inner.total_stake);\n            let right = staker.stake.saturating_mul(u128::MAX);\n\n            let eligible = left < right;\n            if eligible {\n                // Keep the lowest hash to break ties deterministically\n                match &mut best_candidate {\n                    None => best_candidate = Some((staker.id.clone(), hash)),\n                    Some((_best_id, best_hash)) => {\n                        if hash < *best_hash {\n                            *best_hash = hash;\n                            *_best_id = staker.id.clone();\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        inner.current_round += 1;\n\n        if let Some((winner, _)) = &best_candidate {\n            self.event_tx\n                .send(StakingEvent::ComposerSelected {\n                    round: inner.current_round,\n                    staker: winner.clone(),\n                })\n                .ok();\n        }\n\n        Ok(best_candidate.map(|(id, _)| id))\n    }\n\n    /// Utility used primarily by tests & admin dashboards.\n    pub async fn snapshot(&self) -> (u128, Vec<Staker>) {\n        let inner = self.inner.read().await;\n        (inner.total_stake, inner.stakers.values().cloned().collect())\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use std::collections::HashSet;\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn test_stake_add_withdraw() {\n        let pool = StakePool::new(Arc::new(Sha256Vrf::new()));\n        pool.add_stake(\"alice\".into(), vec![1, 2, 3], 1_000).await.unwrap();\n        pool.add_stake(\"bob\".into(), vec![4, 5, 6], 2_000).await.unwrap();\n        let (total, _) = pool.snapshot().await;\n        assert_eq!(total, 3_000);\n\n        pool.withdraw_stake(\"bob\", 500).await.unwrap();\n        let (total, stakers) = pool.snapshot().await;\n        assert_eq!(total, 2_500);\n\n        let bob_stake = stakers.iter().find(|s| s.id == \"bob\").unwrap().stake;\n        assert_eq!(bob_stake, 1_500);\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn test_composer_selection() {\n        let pool = StakePool::new(Arc::new(Sha256Vrf::new()));\n        // Ensure deterministic test by using static VRF keys\n        pool.add_stake(\"alice\".into(), vec![1; 32], 1_000).await.unwrap();\n        pool.add_stake(\"bob\".into(), vec![2; 32], 10_000).await.unwrap();\n\n        let seed = [42u8; 32];\n        let winner = pool.select_composer(seed).await.unwrap().unwrap();\n        assert!([\"alice\", \"bob\"].contains(&winner.as_str()));\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn test_event_broadcast() {\n        let pool = StakePool::new(Arc::new(Sha256Vrf::new()));\n        let mut rx = pool.subscribe();\n\n        pool.add_stake(\"carol\".into(), vec![1; 32], 5_000).await.unwrap();\n\n        let event = rx.recv().await.unwrap();\n        if let StakingEvent::StakeAdded { staker, amount, .. } = event {\n            assert_eq!(staker, \"carol\");\n            assert_eq!(amount, 5_000);\n        } else {\n            panic!(\"unexpected event variant\");\n        }\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test(flavor = \"multi_thread\")]\n    async fn test_multiple_rounds_no_panic() {\n        let pool = Arc::new(StakePool::new(Arc::new(Sha256Vrf::new())));\n        pool.add_stake(\"dave\".into(), vec![9; 32], 15_000).await.unwrap();\n\n        let sp = pool.clone();\n        tokio::spawn(async move {\n            sp.run_composer_election(Duration::from_millis(200))\n                .await;\n        });\n\n        // Wait for a few rounds\n        time::sleep(Duration::from_secs(1)).await;\n        let round = pool.current_round().await;\n        assert!(round >= 3);\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn test_unique_event_order() {\n        let pool = StakePool::new(Arc::new(Sha256Vrf::new()));\n\n        // subscribe *before* any event\n        let mut rx = pool.subscribe();\n\n        pool.add_stake(\"eve\".into(), vec![0; 32],           kinds.insert(std::mem::discriminant(&ev));\n        }\n        assert_eq!(kinds.len(), 2); // received two distinct event types\n    }\n}\n```",

BadRequest(String),\n    NotFound(String),\n    Upstream(GrpcStatus), // error from micro-service\n    Transport(tonic::transport::Error),\n    Unexpected(anyhow::Error),\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for ApiError {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n        use ApiError::*;\n\n        match self {\n            BadRequest(msg) | NotFound(msg) => write!(f, \"{msg}\"),\n            Upstream(status)                => write!(f, \"{status}\"),\n            Transport(err)                  => write!(f, \"{err}\"),\n            Unexpected(err)                 => write!(f, \"{err}\"),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl std::error::Error for ApiError {}\n\nimpl From<GrpcStatus> for ApiError {\n    fn from(value: GrpcStatus) -> Self {\n        ApiError::Upstream(value)\n {\n    fn from(value: anyhow::Error) -> Self {\n        ApiError::Unexpected(value)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Serialises `ApiError` into an RFC7807 compliant JSON payload.\n/// All unrecognised errors are mapped to `500 Internal Server Error` in order\n/// to avoid bleeding sensitive information.\nimpl IntoResponse for ApiError {\n    fn into_response(self) -> Response {\n        let (status, title) = tonic::Code::InvalidArgument=> (StatusCode::BAD_REQUEST, \"Bad Request\"),\n                    _                           => (StatusCode::BAD_GATEWAY, \"Upstream Failure\"),\n                }\n            }\n            _ => (StatusCode::INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR, \"Internal Server Error\"),\n        };\n\n        let problem = serde_json::json!({\n            \"type\":   \"about:blank\",\n            \"title\":  title,\n            \"status\": status.as_u16(),\n            \"detail\": self.to_string(),\n        });\n\n        (status, Json(problem)).into_response()\n    }\n}\n\n// parallel.\n    let mut set = JoinSet::new();\n\n    let cloned = state.clone();\n    set.spawn(async move { cloned.minting.health_check(()).await });\n    let cloned = state.clone();\n \"status\": status })))\n}\n\n#[instrument(name = \"mint_nft\", skip(state, headers, payload))]\nasync fn mint_nft(\n    State(state): State<AppState>,\n    headers: HeaderMap,\n    Json(payload): It is used by mobile wallets, web dApps and the\n// internal orchestration layer.  All monetary values are expressed as\n// unsigned 128-bit integers in the smallest denomination (e.g. wei, \u03bb).\n//\n// NOTE: Never make breaking changes to published fields.  Use field\n// reservations and versioned packages instead.\n\nimport \"google/protobuf/any.proto\";\nimport \"google/protobuf/empty.proto\";\nimport \"google/protobuf/timestamp.proto\";\nimport \"google/protobuf/field_mask.proto\";\nimport \"google/protobuf/wrappers.proto\";\n\noption csharp_namespace   = \"CanvasChain.Marketplace.V1\";\noption go_package         = \"github.com/canvaschain/symphony/ccs_proto/gen/marketplace;marketplacepb\";\noption java_multiple_files = true;\noption java_outer_classname = \"MarketplaceProto\";\noption objc_class_prefix  = \"CCSMarketplace\";\noption php_namespace      = \"CanvasChain\\\\Marketplace\\\\V1\";\n\n//--------------------------------------------------------------------\n// ENUMS\n//--------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nenum Currency {\n  // Default / unknown currency.\n  CURRENCY_UNSPECIFIED = 0;\n  // Native CanvasChain token (e.g. CCS).\n  CURRENCY_NATIVE      = 1;\n  // ERC-20 compatible staking token (e.g. NOTE).\n  CURRENCY_STAKING     = 2;\n  // Stable-coin bridged from Cosmos zone (e.g. axlUSDC).\n  CURRENCY_STABLE      = 3;\n}\n\n// Built-in reason codes for a listing termination.\nenum CloseReason {\n  CLOSE_REASON_UNSPECIFIED = 0;\n  CLOSE_REASON_CANCELLED   = 1;  // Seller cancelled before any match.\n  CLOSE_REASON_SOLD        = 2;  // Listing sold via buy-now or accepted bid.\n  CLOSE_REASON_EXPIRED     = 3;  // Listing expired naturally.\n}\n\n//--------------------------------------------------------------------\n// COMMON TYPES\n//--------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nmessage Money {\n  // Amount in smallest denomination (unsigned 128-bit).\n  uint64 high = 1;  // high 64 bits\n  uint64 low  = 2;  // low  64 bits\n  Currency currency = 3;\n}\n\nmessage Pagination {\n  uint32 limit  = 1;\n  google.protobuf.StringValue cursor = 2; // Opaque, RFC-4648 base64.\n}\n\nmessage PaginationResult {\n  google.protobuf.StringValue next_cursor = 1;\n  uint32 total_count = 2;                 // UUIDv7 for UX, unique per chain.\n  NftId  nft        = 2;\n  string seller     = 3;                 // Chain address of seller.\n  Money  ask_price  = 4;                 // If zero, listing is \u201cauction-only\u201d.\n  repeated Bid bids = 5;                 // Snapshot, omitted in pagination.\n  google.protobuf.Timestamp created_at = 6;\n  google.protobuf.Timestamp expires_at = 7; // 0 = never\n  bool   is_active  = 8;\n  Attributes meta   = 9; // Bids can expire.\n}\n\n//--------------------------------------------------------------------\n// EVENTS (STREAMING)\n//--------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nmessage TradeEvent {\n  oneof payload {\n    ListingCreated created  = 1;\n    ListingClosed  closed   = 2;\n    BidPlaced      bid      = 3;\n    BidAccepted    accepted = 4;\n  }\n\n  google.protobuf.Timestamp timestamp = 10;\n}\n\nmessage ListingCreated {\n  Listing listing = 1;\n}\n\nmessage ListingClosed {\n  string listing_id = 1;\n  CloseReason reason = 2;\n  string buyer = 3; // present when reason == SOLD\n  Money sale_price = 4; // present when reason == SOLD\n}\n\nmessage BidPlaced {\n  Bid bid = 1;\n}\n\nmessage BidAccepted {\n  string bid_id    = 1;\n  string listing_id = 2;\n  Money  sale_price = 3;\n}\n\n//--------------------------------------------------------------------\n// REQUEST / RESPONSE MESSAGES\n//--------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nmessage ListNftRequest {\n  NftId nft      = 1;\n  Money ask_price = 2;          // optional, 0 for auction-only\n  google.protobuf.Timestamp expires_at = 3;\n  Attributes meta = 4;\n}\n\nmessage ListNftResponse {\n  Listing listing = 1;\n}\n\nmessage CancelListingRequest {\n  string listing_id = 1;\n}\n\nmessage CancelListingResponse {\n  Listing listing = 1;          // Closed listing snapshot.\n}\n\nmessage BuyNowRequest {\n  string listing_id = 1;\n}\n\nmessage BuyNowResponse {\n  Listing listing = 1;          // Closed listing snapshot.\n}\n\nmessage PlaceBidRequest {\n  string listing_id = 1;\n  Money  amount     = 2;\n  google.protobuf.Timestamp expires_at = 3;\n}\n\nmessage PlaceBidResponse {\n  Bid bid = 1;\n}\n\nmessage AcceptBidRequest {\n  string bid_id = 1;\n}\n\nmessage AcceptBidResponse {\n  Listing listing = 1;          // Closed listing snapshot.\n}\n\nmessage GetListingRequest {\n  string listing_id = 1;\n  google.protobuf.FieldMask field_mask = 98; // Sparse responses.\n}\n\nmessage GetListingResponse {\n  Listing listing = 1;\n}\n\nmessage QueryListingsRequest {\n  // Filter criteria (AND-ed).  Empty = all active listings.\n  repeated NftId nft_ids = 1;\n  repeated string seller_addrs = 2;\n  Currency currency = 3;\n  google.protobuf.Timestamp newer_than = 4;\n  bool include_inactive = 5;\n  Pagination paging = 99;\n}\n\nmessage QueryListingsResponse {\n  repeated Listing listings = 1;\n  PaginationResult paging = 2;\n}\n\nmessage StreamEventsRequest {\n  // All fields are optional filters.\n  google.protobuf.Timestamp from = 1; // exclusive\n  google.protobuf.Timestamp to   = 2; // inclusive\n  repeated string seller_addrs = 3;\n  repeated string bidder_addrs = 4;\n}\n\n//--------------------------------------------------------------------\n// SERVICE DEFINITION\n//--------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nservice MarketplaceService {\n  // List an NFT for sale or auction.\n  rpc ListNft(ListNftRequest) returns (ListNftResponse);\n\n  // Cancel a listing if it has no accepted bids / sale.\n  rpc CancelListing(CancelListingRequest) returns (CancelListingResponse);\n\n  // Immediate purchase (buy-now) at the ask price.\n  rpc BuyNow(BuyNowRequest) returns (BuyNowResponse);\n\n  // Place or update a bid on a listing.\n  rpc PlaceBid(PlaceBidRequest) returns (PlaceBidResponse);\n\n  // Seller accepts a specific bid; finalizes the trade.\n  rpc AcceptBid(AcceptBidRequest) returns (AcceptBidResponse);\n\n  // Fetch a single listing.\n  rpc GetListing(GetListingRequest) returns (GetListingResponse) {\n    option idempotency_level = IDEMPOTENT;\n  }\n\n  // Query multiple listings with pagination.\n  rpc QueryListings(QueryListingsRequest) returns (QueryListingsResponse) {\n    option idempotency_level = IDEMPOTENT;\n  }\n\n  // Subscribe to marketplace events (server streaming).\n  rpc StreamEvents(StreamEventsRequest) returns (stream TradeEvent);\n}\n\n//--------------------------------------------------------------------\n// RESERVATIONS (prevent accidental reuse of tag numbers)\n//--------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nmessage ListNftRequest {\n  reserved 5 to 20;\n}\n\nmessage CancelListingRequest {\n  reserved 2 to 20;\n}\n\nmessage BuyNowRequest {\n  reserved 2 to 20;\n}\n\nmessage QueryListingsRequest {\n  reserved 6 to 98;\n}",
    "filePath": "/app/project/crates/ccs_proto/proto/marketplace.proto",

{
  "content": "# Fractional NFT (F-NFT) Integration: Technical Design Document\n\n## CanvasChain Symphony Platform\n\n**Document Version:** 1.0\n**Date:** 2026-02-02\n**Author:** Lead Architect\n**Status:** Draft for Review\n\n---\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Executive Summary](#1-executive-summary)\n2. [Impact Analysis](#2-impact-analysis)\n3. [Data Model Changes](#3-data-model-changes)\n4. [Component-Level Design](#4-component-level-design)\n5. [Core User Flows](#5-core-user-flows)\n6. [API & Configuration Changes](#6-api--configuration-changes)\n7. [Event Bus Integration](#7-event-bus-integration)\n8. [Security Considerations](#8-security-considerations)\n9. [Migration Strategy](#9-migration-strategy)\n10. [Appendix: Sequence Diagrams](#10-appendix-sequence-diagrams)\n\n---\n\n## 1. Executive Summary\n\n### 1.1 Feature Overview\n\nFractional NFTs (F-NFTs) enable a single, high-value NFT to be \"sharded\" into multiple fungible tokens representing partial ownership. This feature aims to:\n\n- **Increase liquidity** for high-value NFTs\n- **Democratize access** to expensive digital art\n- **Enable collective ownership** and governance of valuable assets\n\n### 1.2 Architectural Approach\n\nThe F-NFT feature will be implemented by:\n\n1. **Extending the core NFT data model** in `ccs_common` with fractional ownership metadata\n2. **Introducing a new transaction type** (`Transaction::Fractionalize`) in the node service state machine\n3. **Creating dedicated gRPC endpoints** in the minting service for fractionalization operations\n4. **Modifying the marketplace** to support fractional share listings and trading\n5. **Updating the governance service** to handle fractional voting power\n6. **Extending the wallet service** to display and manage fractional holdings\n\n---\n\n## 2. Impact Analysis\n\n### 2.1 Impacted Services\n\n| Service | Impact Level | Description |\n|---------|--------------|-------------|\n| **node_service** | HIGH | New transaction types, state machine changes |\n| **minting_service** | HIGH | Core fractionalization logic, new gRPC endpoints |\n| **marketplace_service** | HIGH | Fractional share trading, listing modifications |\n| **wallet_service** | MEDIUM | Display fractional holdings, balance queries |\n| **governance_service** | MEDIUM | Fractional voting power calculations |\n| **royalty_service** | MEDIUM | Pro-rata royalty distribution to fraction holders |\n| **staking_service** | LOW | Stake-weighted calculations for F-NFT holders |\n| **api_gateway** | MEDIUM | New REST endpoints, gRPC client updates |\n\n### 2.2 Impacted Shared Crates\n\n| Crate | Files Affected | Changes Required |\n|-------|----------------|------------------|\n| **ccs_common** | `src/nft.rs` | New `FractionalInfo` struct, `NftState::Fractionalized` variant |\n| **ccs_proto** | `proto/minting.proto`, `proto/marketplace.proto`, new `proto/fractional.proto` | New message types, RPC definitions |\n| **ccs_db** | `src/state_db.rs` | New tables for fractional shares, ownership mapping |\n| **ccs_consensus** | `src/transaction.rs` | New `Fractionalize`, `RedeemFraction` transaction types |\n\n### 2.3 Critical Files to Modify\n\n#### Core Abstractions (Foundation Layer)\n- `/app/project/crates/ccs_common/src/nft.rs:271-411` - `MultiLayerNft` struct and `NftBuilder`\n- `/app/project/services/node_service/src/state_machine.rs:165-182` - `NodeEvent` enum\n- `/app/project/crates/ccs_proto/proto/common.proto` - Shared protobuf definitions\n\n#### Service-Specific Changes\n- `/app/project/services/minting_service/src/logic/nft_factory.rs:156-264` - `NftFactory` struct\n- `/app/project/services/marketplace_service/src/listing_manager.rs:36-74` - `Listing` struct\n- `/app/project/services/marketplace_service/src/auction_engine.rs:117-135` - `Auction` struct\n- `/app/project/services/wallet_service/src/rpc_server.rs:86-104` - `WalletBackend` trait\n- `/app/project/services/governance_service/src/proposal_engine.rs:66-77` - `Proposal` struct and voting logic\n- `/app/project/services/staking_service/src/staking_logic.rs:79-97` - `Staker` struct\n\n#### API Gateway\n- `/app/project/services/api_gateway/src/rest_api.rs:87-98` - Router configuration\n- `/app/project/services/api_gateway/src/grpc_client.rs:49-60` - `ServiceTarget` enum\n- `/app/project/docs/api/gateway_openapi.yaml` - Changes\n\n**File:** `/app/project/crates/ccs_db/src/state_db.rs`\n\nNew tables required:\n\n```sql\n-- Fractional share tokens\nCREATE TABLE fractional_tokens (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY,\n    parent_nft_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES nfts(id),\n    total_supply NUMERIC(78, 0) NOT NULL,\n    symbol VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL UNIQUE,\n    decimals SMALLINT NOT NULL DEFAULT 18,\n    governance_threshold NUMERIC(78, 0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,\n    reserve_price_per_share NUMERIC(78, 0),\n    auction_duration_secs BIGINT,\n    approval_quorum_bp SMALLINT,\n    vault_address VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,\n    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),\n    reconstituted_at TIMESTAMPTZ,\n    CONSTRAINT valid_decimals CHECK (decimals >= 0 AND decimals <= 18)\n);\n\n-- Fractional ownership records\nCREATE TABLE fractional_holdings (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n    holder_address VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,\n    share_token_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES fractional_tokens(id),\n    amount NUMERIC(78, 0) NOT NULL,\n    locked_amount NUMERIC(78, 0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,\n    acquired_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),\n    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),\n    UNIQUE(holder_address, share_token_id)\n);\n\n-- Fractional transfer history\nCREATE TABLE fractional_transfers (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n    share_token_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES fractional_tokens(id),\n    from_address VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,\n    to_address VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,\n    amount NUMERIC(78, 0) NOT NULL,\n    tx_hash VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,\n    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()\n);\n\n-- Buyout proposals\nCREATE TABLE buyout_proposals (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n    share_token_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES fractional_tokens(id),\n    proposer_address VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,\n    price_per_share NUMERIC(78, 0) NOT NULL,\n    status VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending',\n    votes_for NUMERIC(78, 0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,\n    votes_against NUMERIC(78, 0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,\n    expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,\n    settled_at TIMESTAMPTZ,\n    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()\n);\n\n-- Indexes for common queries\nCREATE INDEX idx_fractional_holdings_holder ON fractional_holdings(holder_address);\nCREATE INDEX idx_fractional_holdings_token ON fractional_holdings(share_token_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_fractional_transfers_token ON fractional_transfers(share_token_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_buyout_proposals_token ON buyout_proposals(share_token_id, status);\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4.
