Verify NFT exists and is owned by requester\n    // 2. Verify NFT is not already fractionalized\n    // 3. Create vault account to hold the NFT\n    // 4. Generate fractional share token\n    // 5. Mint total_shares to the owner\n    // 6. Update NFT state to Fractionalized\n    // 7. Emit FractionalizationCompleted event\n\n    let result = ctx.db.fractionalize_nft(\n        nft_id,\n        owner,\n        total_shares,\n        share_symbol,\n        buyout_config\n    ).await?;\n\n    ctx.bus.publish(NodeEvent::FractionalizationCompleted(result))\n        .await\n        .map_err(|e| anyhow::anyhow!(\"failed to publish event: {e}\"))?;\n\n    Ok(Transition::Stay)\n}\n```\n\n### 4.2 Minting Service Changes\n\n**File:** `/app/project/services/minting_service/src/logic/nft_factory.rs`\n\n#### 4.2.1 New Request/Response Types\n\n```rust\n// Add after line 70\n\n/// Request to fractionalize an existing NFT\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct FractionalizeRequest {\n    /// ID of the NFT to fractionalize\n    pub nft_id: Uuid,\n    /// Wallet address of the current owner\n    pub owner_wallet: String,\n    /// Number of fractional shares to create\n    pub total_shares: u128,\n    /// Symbol for the fractional token (e.g., \"MONA-F\")\n    pub share_symbol: String,\n    /// Minimum shares needed for governance participation\n    pub governance_threshold: u128,\n    /// Buyout configuration\n    pub buyout_config: BuyoutConfigRequest,\n    /// Nonce for replay protection\n    pub nonce: u64,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct BuyoutConfigRequest {\n    /// Reserve price per share in smallest token denomination\n    pub reserve_price_per_share: u128,\n    /// Auction duration in seconds\n    pub auction_duration_secs: u64,\n    /// Approval quorum in basis points (e.g., 5000 = 50%)\n    pub approval_quorum_bp: u16,\n}\n\n/// Response from fractionalization\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct FractionalizeResponse {\n    /// ID of the created fractional share token\n    pub share_token_id: Uuid,\n    /// Transaction hash\n    pub tx_hash: String,\n    /// Vault address holding the original NFT\n    pub vault_address: String,\n    /// Total shares created\n    pub total_shares: u128,\n}\n```\n\n#### 4.2.2 New Factory Methods\n\n```rust\n// Add to NftFactory impl\n\n/// Fractionalize an existing NFT into fungible share tokens\n#[instrument(skip_all, level = \"info\", fields(nft_id = %req.nft_id))]\npub async fn fractionalize_nft(\n    &self,\n    req: FractionalizeRequest,\n) -> Result<FractionalizeResponse, FactoryError> {\n    // 1. Validate request\n    self.validate_fractionalize_request(&req)?;\n\n    // 2. Verify ownership via chain query\n    let nft = self.chain.get_nft(req.nft_id).await\n        .map_err(|e| FactoryError::Blockchain(e))?;\n\n    if nft.owner != req.owner_wallet {\n        return Err(FactoryError::Validation(\n            \"Only NFT owner can fractionalize\".into()\n        ));\n    }\n\n    // 3. Generate vault address for escrowing the NFT\n    let vault_address = self.generate_vault_address(&req.nft_id)?;\n\n    // 4. Build fractionalization payload\n    let share_token_id = Uuid::new_v4();\n    let payload = FractionalizePayload {\n        nft_id: req.nft_id,\n        share_token_id,\n        total_shares: req.total_shares,\n        share_symbol: req.share_symbol.clone(),\n        vault_address: vault_address.clone(),\n        buyout_config: req.buyout_config.clone(),\n        owner: req.owner_wallet.clone(),\n        nonce: req.nonce,\n    };\n\n    // 5. Sign the payload\n    let payload_bytes = self.serialize_fractionalize_payload(&payload)?;\n    let signature = self.signer.sign(&payload_bytes).await?;\n\n    // 6. Submit to chain\n    let tx_hash = self.chain.submit_fractionalize(payload, signature).await?;\n\n    // 7. Publish success event\n    self.bus.publish(\n        &self.config.event_topic_fractionalize,\n        &FractionalizeEvent {\n            nft_id: req.nft_id,\n            share_token_id,\n            total_shares: req.total_shares,\n            vault_address: vault_address.clone(),\n            tx_hash: tx_hash.clone(),\n        }\n    ).await?;\n\n    info!(\n        share_token_id = %share_token_id,\n        tx_hash = %tx_hash,\n        \"NFT fractionalized successfully\"\n    );\n\n    Ok(FractionalizeResponse {\n        share_token_id,\n        tx_hash,\n        vault_address,\n        total_shares: req.total_shares,\n    })\n}\n\nfn validate_fractionalize_request(&self, req: &FractionalizeRequest) -> Result<(), FactoryError> {\n    if req.total_shares == 0 {\n        return Err(FactoryError::Validation(\"total_shares must be > 0\".into()));\n    }\n    if req.total_shares > 1_000_000_000_000 {\n        return Err(FactoryError::Validation(\"total_shares exceeds maximum\".into()));\n    }\n    if req.share_symbol.is_empty() || req.share_symbol.len() > 12 {\n        return Err(FactoryError::Validation(\"invalid share_symbol\".into()));\n    }\n    if req.buyout_config.approval_quorum_bp > 10_000 {\n        return Err(FactoryError::Validation(\"invalid quorum percentage\".into()));\n    }\n    Ok(())\n}\n```\n\n### 4.3 Marketplace Service pub token_id: String,\n    pub price: Decimal,\n    pub status: ListingStatus,\n    pub created_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n    pub updated_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n    // NEW: Listing type\n    pub listing_type: impl\n\n/// Create a listing for fractional NFT shares\n#[instrument(skip(self))]\npub async fn create_fractional_listing(\n    &self,\n    owner: AccountId,\n    share_token_id: Uuid,\n    shares_amount: u128,\n    price_per_share: Decimal,\n) -> Result<ListingId, ListingError> {\n    // Validate the seller owns the shares\n    // (This would involve a call to the wallet service or chain query)\n\n    let total_price = price_per_share * Decimal::from(shares_amount);\n\n    let listing = Listing {\n        id: ListingId::new(),\n        owner,\n        nft_contract: String::new(), // Not applicable for fractional\n        token_id: share_token_id.to_string(),\n        price: total_price,\n        status: ListingStatus::Active,\n        created_at: Utc::now(),\n        updated_at: Utc::now(),\n        listing_type: ListingType::FractionalShares {\n            share_token_id,\n            shares_amount,\n        },\n        price_per_share: Some(price_per_share),\n    };\n\n    timeout(DB_OP_TIMEOUT, self.repo.insert(listing.clone()))\n        .await\n        .map_err(|_| ListingError::Timeout)??;\n\n    self.dispatch_event(MarketplaceEvent::FractionalListingCreated {\n        listing_id: listing.id,\n        share_token_id,\n        shares_amount,\n        price_per_share,\n    })?;\n\n    Ok(listing.id)\n}\n\n/// Purchase fractional shares from a listing\n#[instrument(skip(self))]\npub async fn purchase_fractional_shares(\n    &self,\n    listing_id: ListingId,\n    buyer: AccountId,\n    shares_to_buy: u128,\n) -> Result<(), ListingError> {\n    let mut listing = timeout(DB_OP_TIMEOUT, self.repo.get(listing_id))\n        .await\n        .map_err(|_| ListingError::Timeout)??;\n\n    // Validate listing is for fractional shares\n    let (share_token_id, available_shares) = match &listing.listing_type {\n        ListingType::FractionalShares { share_token_id, shares_amount } => {\n            (*share_token_id, *shares_amount)\n        }\n        _ => return Err(ListingError::NotFractionalListing),\n    };\n\n    if shares_to_buy > available_shares {\n        return Err(ListingError::InsufficientShares);\n    }\n\n    // Calculate payment\n    let price_per_share = listing.price_per_share\n        .ok_or(ListingError::Repository(\"missing price_per_share\".into()))?;\n    let payment = price_per_share * Decimal::from(shares_to_buy);\n\n    // Update listing (partial fill support)\n    let remaining_shares = available_shares - shares_to_buy;\n    if remaining_shares == 0 {\n        listing.status = ListingStatus::Sold;\n    } else {\n        listing.listing_type = ListingType::FractionalShares {\n            share_token_id,\n            shares_amount: remaining_shares,\n        };\n        listing.price = price_per_share * Decimal::from(remaining_shares);\n    }\n    listing.updated_at = Utc::now();\n\n    timeout(DB_OP_TIMEOUT, self.repo.update(listing.clone()))\n        .await\n        .map_err(|_| ListingError::Timeout)??;\n\n    self.dispatch_event(MarketplaceEvent::FractionalSharesPurchased {\n        listing_id,\n        buyer,\n        share_token_id,\n        shares_amount: shares_to_buy,\n        total_price: payment,\n    })?;\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n```\n\n**File:** `/app/project/services/marketplace_service/src/auction_engine.rs`\n\n#### 4.3.3 Extend Auction Engine\n\n```rust\n// Modify CreateAuction struct (line 93)\n\n#[derive(Debug)]\npub struct CreateAuction Fractional Voting Power\n\n```rust\n// Add new voting power calculator\n\n/// Calculate voting power for fractional NFT holders\npub fn calculate_fractional_voting_power(\n    share_token_id: Uuid,\n    voter_shares: u128,\n    total_shares: u128,\n    base_voting_power: u64,\n) -> u64 {\n    if total_shares == 0 {\n        return 0;\n    }\n\n    // Voting power is proportional to share ownership\n    // scaled by the base voting power of the whole NFT\n    let share_ratio = voter_shares as f64 / total_shares as f64;\n    (base_voting_power as f64 * share_ratio) as u64\n}\n\n// Modify cast_vote method to handle fractional voting\npub async fn cast_vote(\n    &self,\n    proposal_id: Uuid,\n    voter: &str,\n    choice: VoteChoice,\n    signature: &[u8],\n    // NEW: Optional fractional voting parameters\n    fractional_vote: Option<FractionalVoteParams>,\n) -> Result<(), ProposalError> {\n    // ... existing signature verification ...\n\n    let voting_power = match fractional_vote {\n        Some(params) => {\n            // Verify voter owns the shares\n            // Calculate proportional voting power\n            calculate_fractional_voting_power(\n                params.share_token_id,\n                params.shares_to_vote,\n                params.total_supply,\n                params.base_voting_power,\n            )\n        }\n        None => {\n            // Standard voting power calculation\n            1 // or based on token holdings\n        }\n    };\n\n    // ... rest of voting logic with weighted power ...\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct FractionalVoteParams {\n    pub share_token_id: Uuid,\n    pub shares_to_vote: u128,\n    pub total_supply: u128,\n    pub base_voting_power: u64,\n}\n```\n\n### 4.6 Staking Service Changes\n\n**File:** `/app/project/services/staking_service/src/staking_logic.rs`\n\n#### 4.6.1 Fractional Stake Tracking\n\n```rust\n// Modify Staker struct (line 79) to include fractional holdings\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct Staker {\n    pub id: StakerId,\n    pub stake: u128,\n    pub last_active: DateTime<Utc>,\n    pub vrf_pubkey: Vec<u8>,\n    // NEW: Fractional NFT holdings that count toward stake\n    pub fractional_stakes: Vec<FractionalStake>,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct FractionalStake {\n    pub share_token_id: Uuid,\n    pub shares_held: u128,\n    /// Stake value derived from share ownership\n    pub stake_value: u128,\n}\n\nimpl Staker {\n    /// Calculate total effective stake including fractional holdings\n    pub fn effective_stake(&self) -> u128 {\n        let fractional_stake: u128 = self.fractional_stakes\n            .iter()\n            .map(|fs| fs.stake_value)\n            .sum();\n\n        self.stake.saturating_add(fractional_stake)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Core User Flows\n\n### 5.1 Flow A: Owner Fractionalizing Their NFT\n\n#### Sequence of Operations\n\n1. **User initiates fractionalization** via API Gateway\n2. **API Gateway** validates request and forwards to Minting Service\n3. **Minting Service** verifies ownership and creates fractionalization payload\n4. **Minting Service** submits transaction to Node Service\n5. **Node Service** validates and processes the transaction:\n   - Creates vault address for NFT escrow\n   - Generates fractional share token\n   - Mints total shares to owner\n   - Updates NFT state to `Fractionalized`\n6. **Node Service** publishes `FractionalizationCompleted` event\n7. **Event listeners** in Wallet, Marketplace, and Governance services update their state\n\n#### Detailed Flow\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510     \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510 specifying listing and share amount\n3. **API Gateway** forwards to Marketplace Service\n4. **Marketplace Service** validates listing and calculates price\n5. **Marketplace Service** initiates payment verification\n6. **Marketplace Service** submits share transfer to Node Service\n7. **Node Service** processes transfer transaction:\n   - Debits shares from seller\n   - Credits shares to buyer\n   - Handles royalty distribution\n8. **Node Service** publishes `SharesTransferred` event\n9. **Wallet Service** updates both buyer and seller balances\n\n#### Detailed Flow\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510     \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510 share_token_id, seller_address, shares_amount, price_per_share]\n\n# Add new paths:\n\n/v1/nfts/{nft_id}/fractionalize:\n  parameters:\n    - name: nft_id\n      in: path\n      required: true\n section:\n\n```toml\n#######################################################################\n# Fractional NFT Configuration\n#######################################################################\n[fractional]\n# Enable/disable F-NFT feature\nenabled = true\n\n# Minimum shares when fractionalizing (prevents dust)\nmin_shares = 100\n\n# Maximum shares when fractionalizing (prevents overflow)\nmax_shares = 1_000_000_000_000\n\n# Default buyout auction duration in seconds (72 hours)\ndefault_auction_duration_secs = 259200\n\n# Default approval quorum in basis points (50%)\ndefault_approval_quorum_bp = 5000\n\n# Minimum reserve price per share in smallest denomination\nmin_reserve_price = 1\n\n# Fee for fractionalization (basis points)\nfractionalization_fee_bp = 25  # 0.25%\n\n# Fee for reconstitution (basis points)\nreconstitution_fee_bp = 50     # 0.5%\n\n# Share symbol prefix\nsymbol_prefix = \"FNFT-\"\n\n# Maximum symbol length\nmax_symbol_length = 12\n\n# Governance threshold default (basis points of total supply)\ndefault_governance_threshold_bp = 100  # 1%\n\n# Event bus topics\n[fractional.events]\nfractionalized = \"nft.fractionalized\"\nshares_transferred = \"nft.shares.transferred\"\nbuyout_initiated = \"nft.buyout.initiated\"\nbuyout_voted = \"nft.buyout.voted\"\nbuyout_executed = \"nft.buyout.executed\"\nreconstituted = \"nft.reconstituted\"\n\n# Rate limiting\n[fractional.rate_limits]\nfractionalize_per_hour = 10\ntransfer_per_minute = 100\nbuyout_per_day = 5\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Event Bus Integration\n\n### 7.1 New NATS Subjects\n\nFollowing the existing subject hierarchy pattern from ADR-002:\n\n```\nnft.fractional.v1.fractionalized     # NFT was fractionalized\nnft.fractional.v1.shares.transferred # Shares transferred between addresses\nnft.fractional.v1.shares.locked      # Shares locked for governance\nnft.fractional.v1.shares.unlocked    # Shares unlocked after vote\nnft.fractional.v1.buyout.initiated   # Buyout proposal created\nnft.fractional.v1.buyout.voted       # Vote cast on buyout\nnft.fractional.v1.buyout.executed    # Buyout completed\nnft.fractional.v1.reconstituted      # NFT reconstituted from shares\n```\n\n### 7.2 Event Payloads\n\n```rust\n// Add to crate event types\n\n#[derive(Clone, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum FractionalEvent {\n    Fractionalized {\n        nft_id: Uuid,\n        share_token_id: Uuid,\n        owner: WalletAddress,\n        total_shares: u128,\n        vault_address: WalletAddress,\n        tx_hash: String,\n        timestamp: u64,\n    },\n\n    SharesTransferred {\n        share_token_id: Uuid,\n        from: WalletAddress,\n        to: WalletAddress,\n        amount: u128,\n        tx_hash: String,\n        timestamp: u64,\n    },\n\n    BuyoutInitiated {\n        proposal_id: Uuid,\n        share_token_id: Uuid,\n        proposer: WalletAddress,\n        price_per_share: TokenAmount,\n        expires_at: u64,\n        tx_hash: String,\n    },\n\n    BuyoutVoted {\n        proposal_id: Uuid,\n        voter: WalletAddress,\n        approve: bool,\n        voting_shares: u128,\n        tx_hash: String,\n    },\n\n    BuyoutExecuted {\n        proposal_id: Uuid,\n        share_token_id: Uuid,\n        winner: WalletAddress,\n        total_price: TokenAmount,\n        tx_hash: String,\n    },\n\n    Reconstituted {\n        share_token_id: Uuid,\n        nft_id: Uuid,\n        redeemer: WalletAddress,\n        tx_hash: String,\n        timestamp: u64,\n    },\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 8. Security Considerations\n\n### 8.1 Attack Vectors & Mitigations\n\n| Attack Vector | Risk | Mitigation |\n|--------------|------|------------|\n| **Sybil voting** | Attacker creates many addresses to game buyout votes | Require minimum governance threshold; weight votes by shares held |\n| **Flash loan attacks** | Borrow shares, vote, return shares | Implement voting lockup period; snapshot-based voting |\n| **Front-running buyouts** | MEV bots front-run buyout execution | Use commit-reveal scheme for buyout proposals |\n| **Dust share attacks** | Create many tiny listings to spam marketplace | Minimum listing size; listing fees |\n| **Oracle manipulation** | Manipulate price feeds affecting buyout pricing | Use TWAP; multi-oracle aggregation |\n| **Reconstitution griefing** | Collect 99.9% shares, block reconstitution | Forced buyout mechanism with supermajority |\n\n### 8.2 Signature Requirements\n\nAll state-changing operations require:\n1. Valid signature from the transaction initiator\n2. Nonce for replay protection\n3. Timestamp within acceptable drift window\n\n### 8.3 Invariants to Enforce\n\n1. **Share supply invariant**: Sum of all holdings must equal total supply\n2. **Locked share invariant**: Locked shares cannot be transferred\n3. **Vault invariant**: NFT must remain in vault while fractionalized\n4. **Reconstitution invariant**: Only holder of 100% shares can reconstitute\n\n---\n\n## 9. Migration Strategy\n\n### 9.1 Database Migration\n\n1. Create new tables with `IF NOT EXISTS` guards\n2. Add `fractionalization` column to existing `nfts` table as nullable JSON\n3. Backfill existing NFTs with `Whole` state\n4. Create indexes for performance\n\n### 9.2 Service Deployment Order\n\n1. **Phase 1**: Deploy `ccs_common` and `ccs_proto` changes\n2. **Phase 2**: Deploy database migrations\n3. **Phase 3**: Deploy `node_service` with new transaction types (feature-flagged)\n4. **Phase 4**: Deploy `minting_service` with fractionalization logic\n5. **Phase 5**: Deploy `marketplace_service`, `wallet_service` updates\n6. **Phase 6**: Deploy `api_gateway` with new endpoints\n7. **Phase 7**: Enable feature flag; monitor for issues\n8. **Phase 8**: Deploy `governance_service`, `staking_service` updates\n\n### 9.3 Feature Flag\n\nAll F-NFT functionality should be gated by a feature flag:\n\n```rust\n// In each service\nif config.fractional.enabled {\n    // Register F-NFT routes/handlers\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 10. Appendix: Sequence Diagrams\n\n### 10.1 Complete Fractionalization Flow\n\n```\nUser        Gateway      Minting      Node       Wallet      EventBus\n \u2502            \u2502            \u2502 platform. Key points:\n\n1. **Foundation**: Changes start in `ccs_common/src/nft.rs` with new data structures and extend to all services\n2. **State Management**: The `node_service` state machine handles all critical state transitions atomically\n3. **Service Communication**: All inter-service calls follow the existing gRPC + NATS patterns per ADR-002\n4. **Security**: Multiple attack vectors are addressed with signature requirements and voting lockups\n5. **Migration**: Phased deployment with feature flags enables safe rollout\n\nThe implementation team should follow the component-level designs closely, ensuring that:\n- All state changes are validated by the consensus nodes\n- Events are published for all significant state transitions\n- The existing architecture patterns (Factory, Strategy, Observer) are maintained\n- Tests are written for each new transaction type and API endpoint\n",

{
  "content": "# Fractional NFT (F-NFT) Integration: Technical Design Document\n\n## CanvasChain Symphony Platform\n\n**Document Version:** 1.0\n**Date:** 2026-02-02\n**Author:** Lead Architect\n**Status:** Draft for Review\n\n---\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Executive Summary](#1-executive-summary)\n2. [Impact Analysis](#2-impact-analysis)\n3. [Data Model Changes](#3-data-model-changes)\n4. [Component-Level Design](#4-component-level-design)\n5. [Core User Flows](#5-core-user-flows)\n6. [API & Configuration Changes](#6-api--configuration-changes)\n7. [Event Bus Integration](#7-event-bus-integration)\n8. [Security Considerations](#8-security-considerations)\n9. [Migration Strategy](#9-migration-strategy)\n10. [Appendix: Sequence Diagrams](#10-appendix-sequence-diagrams)\n\n---\n\n## 1. Executive Summary\n\n### 1.1 Feature Overview\n\nFractional NFTs (F-NFTs) enable a single, high-value NFT to be \"sharded\" into multiple fungible tokens representing partial ownership. This feature aims to:\n\n- **Increase liquidity** for high-value NFTs\n- **Democratize access** to expensive digital art\n- **Enable collective ownership** and governance of valuable assets\n\n### 1.2 Architectural Approach\n\nThe F-NFT feature will be implemented by:\n\n1. **Extending the core NFT data model** in `ccs_common` with fractional ownership metadata\n2. **Introducing a new transaction type** (`Transaction::Fractionalize`) in the node service state machine\n3. **Creating dedicated gRPC endpoints** in the minting service for fractionalization operations\n4. **Modifying the marketplace** to support fractional share listings and trading\n5. **Updating the governance service** to handle fractional voting power\n6. **Extending the wallet service** to display and manage fractional holdings\n\n---\n\n## 2. Impact Analysis\n\n### 2.1 Impacted Services\n\n| Service | Impact Level | Description |\n|---------|--------------|-------------|\n| **node_service** | HIGH | New transaction types, state machine changes |\n| **minting_service** | HIGH | Core fractionalization logic, new gRPC endpoints |\n| **marketplace_service** | HIGH | Fractional share trading, listing modifications |\n| **wallet_service** | MEDIUM | Display fractional holdings, balance queries |\n| **governance_service** | MEDIUM | Fractional voting power calculations |\n| **royalty_service** | MEDIUM | Pro-rata royalty distribution to fraction holders |\n| **staking_service** | LOW | Stake-weighted calculations for F-NFT holders |\n| **api_gateway** | MEDIUM | New REST endpoints, gRPC client updates |\n\n### 2.2 Impacted Shared Crates\n\n| Crate | Files Affected | Changes Required |\n|-------|----------------|------------------|\n| **ccs_common** | `src/nft.rs` | New `FractionalInfo` struct, `NftState::Fractionalized` variant |\n| **ccs_proto** | `proto/minting.proto`, `proto/marketplace.proto`, new `proto/fractional.proto` | New message types, RPC definitions |\n| **ccs_db** | `src/state_db.rs` | New tables for fractional shares, ownership mapping |\n| **ccs_consensus** | `src/transaction.rs` | New `Fractionalize`, `RedeemFraction` transaction types |\n\n### 2.3 Critical Files to Modify\n\n#### Core Abstractions (Foundation Layer)\n- `/app/project/crates/ccs_common/src/nft.rs:271-411` - `MultiLayerNft` struct and `NftBuilder`\n- `/app/project/services/node_service/src/state_machine.rs:165-182` - `NodeEvent` enum\n- `/app/project/crates/ccs_proto/proto/common.proto` - Shared protobuf definitions\n\n#### Service-Specific Changes\n- `/app/project/services/minting_service/src/logic/nft_factory.rs:156-264` - `NftFactory` struct\n- `/app/project/services/marketplace_service/src/listing_manager.rs:36-74` - `Listing` struct\n- `/app/project/services/marketplace_service/src/auction_engine.rs:117-135` - `Auction` struct\n- `/app/project/services/wallet_service/src/rpc_server.rs:86-104` - `WalletBackend` trait\n- `/app/project/services/governance_service/src/proposal_engine.rs:66-77` - `Proposal` struct and voting logic\n- `/app/project/services/staking_service/src/staking_logic.rs:79-97` - `Staker` struct\n\n#### API Gateway\n- `/app/project/services/api_gateway/src/rest_api.rs:87-98` - Router configuration\n- `/app/project/services/api_gateway/src/grpc_client.rs:49-60` - `ServiceTarget` enum\n- `/app/project/docs/api/gateway_openapi.yaml` - Changes\n\n**File:** `/app/project/crates/ccs_db/src/state_db.rs`\n\nNew tables required:\n\n```sql\n-- Fractional share tokens\nCREATE TABLE fractional_tokens (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY,\n    parent_nft_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES nfts(id),\n    total_supply NUMERIC(78, 0) NOT NULL,\n    symbol VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL UNIQUE,\n    decimals SMALLINT NOT NULL DEFAULT 18,\n    governance_threshold NUMERIC(78, 0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,\n    reserve_price_per_share NUMERIC(78, 0),\n    auction_duration_secs BIGINT,\n    approval_quorum_bp SMALLINT,\n    vault_address VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,\n    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),\n    reconstituted_at TIMESTAMPTZ,\n    CONSTRAINT valid_decimals CHECK (decimals >= 0 AND decimals <= 18)\n);\n\n-- Fractional ownership records\nCREATE TABLE fractional_holdings (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n    holder_address VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,\n    share_token_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES fractional_tokens(id),\n    amount NUMERIC(78, 0) NOT NULL,\n    locked_amount NUMERIC(78, 0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,\n    acquired_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),\n    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),\n    UNIQUE(holder_address, share_token_id)\n);\n\n-- Fractional transfer history\nCREATE TABLE fractional_transfers (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n    share_token_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES fractional_tokens(id),\n    from_address VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,\n    to_address VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,\n    amount NUMERIC(78, 0) NOT NULL,\n    tx_hash VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,\n    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()\n);\n\n-- Buyout proposals\nCREATE TABLE buyout_proposals (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n    share_token_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES fractional_tokens(id),\n    proposer_address VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,\n    price_per_share NUMERIC(78, 0) NOT NULL,\n    status VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending',\n    votes_for NUMERIC(78, 0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,\n    votes_against NUMERIC(78, 0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,\n    expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,\n    settled_at TIMESTAMPTZ,\n    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()\n);\n\n-- Indexes for common queries\nCREATE INDEX idx_fractional_holdings_holder ON fractional_holdings(holder_address);\nCREATE INDEX idx_fractional_holdings_token ON fractional_holdings(share_token_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_fractional_transfers_token ON fractional_transfers(share_token_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_buyout_proposals_token ON buyout_proposals(share_token_id, status);\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Verify NFT exists and is owned by requester\n    // 2. Verify NFT is not already fractionalized\n    // 3. Create vault account to hold the NFT\n    // 4. Generate fractional share token\n    // 5. Mint total_shares to the owner\n    // 6. Update NFT state to Fractionalized\n    // 7. Emit FractionalizationCompleted event\n\n    let result = ctx.db.fractionalize_nft(\n        nft_id,\n        owner,\n        total_shares,\n        share_symbol,\n        buyout_config\n    ).await?;\n\n    ctx.bus.publish(NodeEvent::FractionalizationCompleted(result))\n        .await\n        .map_err(|e| anyhow::anyhow!(\"failed to publish event: {e}\"))?;\n\n    Ok(Transition::Stay)\n}\n```\n\n### 4.2 Minting Service Changes\n\n**File:** `/app/project/services/minting_service/src/logic/nft_factory.rs`\n\n#### 4.2.1 New Request/Response Types\n\n```rust\n// Add after line 70\n\n/// Request to fractionalize an existing NFT\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct FractionalizeRequest {\n    /// ID of the NFT to fractionalize\n    pub nft_id: Uuid,\n    /// Wallet address of the current owner\n    pub owner_wallet: String,\n    /// Number of fractional shares to create\n    pub total_shares: u128,\n    /// Symbol for the fractional token (e.g., \"MONA-F\")\n    pub share_symbol: String,\n    /// Minimum shares needed for governance participation\n    pub governance_threshold: u128,\n    /// Buyout configuration\n    pub buyout_config: BuyoutConfigRequest,\n    /// Nonce for replay protection\n    pub nonce: u64,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct BuyoutConfigRequest {\n    /// Reserve price per share in smallest token denomination\n    pub reserve_price_per_share: u128,\n    /// Auction duration in seconds\n    pub auction_duration_secs: u64,\n    /// Approval quorum in basis points (e.g., 5000 = 50%)\n    pub approval_quorum_bp: u16,\n}\n\n/// Response from fractionalization\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct FractionalizeResponse {\n    /// ID of the created fractional share token\n    pub share_token_id: Uuid,\n    /// Transaction hash\n    pub tx_hash: String,\n    /// Vault address holding the original NFT\n    pub vault_address: String,\n    /// Total shares created\n    pub total_shares: u128,\n}\n```\n\n#### 4.2.2 New Factory Methods\n\n```rust\n// Add to NftFactory impl\n\n/// Fractionalize an existing NFT into fungible share tokens\n#[instrument(skip_all, level = \"info\", fields(nft_id = %req.nft_id))]\npub async fn fractionalize_nft(\n    &self,\n    req: FractionalizeRequest,\n) -> Result<FractionalizeResponse, FactoryError> {\n    // 1. Validate request\n    self.validate_fractionalize_request(&req)?;\n\n    // 2. Verify ownership via chain query\n    let nft = self.chain.get_nft(req.nft_id).await\n        .map_err(|e| FactoryError::Blockchain(e))?;\n\n    if nft.owner != req.owner_wallet {\n        return Err(FactoryError::Validation(\n            \"Only NFT owner can fractionalize\".into()\n        ));\n    }\n\n    // 3. Generate vault address for escrowing the NFT\n    let vault_address = self.generate_vault_address(&req.nft_id)?;\n\n    // 4. Build fractionalization payload\n    let share_token_id = Uuid::new_v4();\n    let payload = FractionalizePayload {\n        nft_id: req.nft_id,\n        share_token_id,\n        total_shares: req.total_shares,\n        share_symbol: req.share_symbol.clone(),\n        vault_address: vault_address.clone(),\n        buyout_config: req.buyout_config.clone(),\n        owner: req.owner_wallet.clone(),\n        nonce: req.nonce,\n    };\n\n    // 5. Sign the payload\n    let payload_bytes = self.serialize_fractionalize_payload(&payload)?;\n    let signature = self.signer.sign(&payload_bytes).await?;\n\n    // 6. Submit to chain\n    let tx_hash = self.chain.submit_fractionalize(payload, signature).await?;\n\n    // 7. Publish success event\n    self.bus.publish(\n        &self.config.event_topic_fractionalize,\n        &FractionalizeEvent {\n            nft_id: req.nft_id,\n            share_token_id,\n            total_shares: req.total_shares,\n            vault_address: vault_address.clone(),\n            tx_hash: tx_hash.clone(),\n        }\n    ).await?;\n\n    info!(\n        share_token_id = %share_token_id,\n        tx_hash = %tx_hash,\n        \"NFT fractionalized successfully\"\n    );\n\n    Ok(FractionalizeResponse {\n        share_token_id,\n        tx_hash,\n        vault_address,\n        total_shares: req.total_shares,\n    })\n}\n\nfn validate_fractionalize_request(&self, req: &FractionalizeRequest) -> Result<(), FactoryError> {\n    if req.total_shares == 0 {\n        return Err(FactoryError::Validation(\"total_shares must be > 0\".into()));\n    }\n    if req.total_shares > 1_000_000_000_000 {\n        return Err(FactoryError::Validation(\"total_shares exceeds maximum\".into()));\n    }\n    if req.share_symbol.is_empty() || req.share_symbol.len() > 12 {\n        return Err(FactoryError::Validation(\"invalid share_symbol\".into()));\n    }\n    if req.buyout_config.approval_quorum_bp > 10_000 {\n        return Err(FactoryError::Validation(\"invalid quorum percentage\".into()));\n    }\n    Ok(())\n}\n```\n\n### 4.3 Marketplace Service pub token_id: String,\n    pub price: Decimal,\n    pub status: ListingStatus,\n    pub created_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n    pub updated_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n    // NEW: Listing type\n    pub listing_type: impl\n\n/// Create a listing for fractional NFT shares\n#[instrument(skip(self))]\npub async fn create_fractional_listing(\n    &self,\n    owner: AccountId,\n    share_token_id: Uuid,\n    shares_amount: u128,\n    price_per_share: Decimal,\n) -> Result<ListingId, ListingError> {\n    // Validate the seller owns the shares\n    // (This would involve a call to the wallet service or chain query)\n\n    let total_price = price_per_share * Decimal::from(shares_amount);\n\n    let listing = Listing {\n        id: ListingId::new(),\n        owner,\n        nft_contract: String::new(), // Not applicable for fractional\n        token_id: share_token_id.to_string(),\n        price: total_price,\n        status: ListingStatus::Active,\n        created_at: Utc::now(),\n        updated_at: Utc::now(),\n        listing_type: ListingType::FractionalShares {\n            share_token_id,\n            shares_amount,\n        },\n        price_per_share: Some(price_per_share),\n    };\n\n    timeout(DB_OP_TIMEOUT, self.repo.insert(listing.clone()))\n        .await\n        .map_err(|_| ListingError::Timeout)??;\n\n    self.dispatch_event(MarketplaceEvent::FractionalListingCreated {\n        listing_id: listing.id,\n        share_token_id,\n        shares_amount,\n        price_per_share,\n    })?;\n\n    Ok(listing.id)\n}\n\n/// Purchase fractional shares from a listing\n#[instrument(skip(self))]\npub async fn purchase_fractional_shares(\n    &self,\n    listing_id: ListingId,\n    buyer: AccountId,\n    shares_to_buy: u128,\n) -> Result<(), ListingError> {\n    let mut listing = timeout(DB_OP_TIMEOUT, self.repo.get(listing_id))\n        .await\n        .map_err(|_| ListingError::Timeout)??;\n\n    // Validate listing is for fractional shares\n    let (share_token_id, available_shares) = match &listing.listing_type {\n        ListingType::FractionalShares { share_token_id, shares_amount } => {\n            (*share_token_id, *shares_amount)\n        }\n        _ => return Err(ListingError::NotFractionalListing),\n    };\n\n    if shares_to_buy > available_shares {\n        return Err(ListingError::InsufficientShares);\n    }\n\n    // Calculate payment\n    let price_per_share = listing.price_per_share\n        .ok_or(ListingError::Repository(\"missing price_per_share\".into()))?;\n    let payment = price_per_share * Decimal::from(shares_to_buy);\n\n    // Update listing (partial fill support)\n    let remaining_shares = available_shares - shares_to_buy;\n    if remaining_shares == 0 {\n        listing.status = ListingStatus::Sold;\n    } else {\n        listing.listing_type = ListingType::FractionalShares {\n            share_token_id,\n            shares_amount: remaining_shares,\n        };\n        listing.price = price_per_share * Decimal::from(remaining_shares);\n    }\n    listing.updated_at = Utc::now();\n\n    timeout(DB_OP_TIMEOUT, self.repo.update(listing.clone()))\n        .await\n        .map_err(|_| ListingError::Timeout)??;\n\n    self.dispatch_event(MarketplaceEvent::FractionalSharesPurchased {\n        listing_id,\n        buyer,\n        share_token_id,\n        shares_amount: shares_to_buy,\n        total_price: payment,\n    })?;\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n```\n\n**File:** `/app/project/services/marketplace_service/src/auction_engine.rs`\n\n#### 4.3.3 Extend Auction Engine\n\n```rust\n// Modify CreateAuction struct (line 93)\n\n#[derive(Debug)]\npub struct CreateAuction Fractional Voting Power\n\n```rust\n// Add new voting power calculator\n\n/// Calculate voting power for fractional NFT holders\npub fn calculate_fractional_voting_power(\n    share_token_id: Uuid,\n    voter_shares: u128,\n    total_shares: u128,\n    base_voting_power: u64,\n) -> u64 {\n    if total_shares == 0 {\n        return 0;\n    }\n\n    // Voting power is proportional to share ownership\n    // scaled by the base voting power of the whole NFT\n    let share_ratio = voter_shares as f64 / total_shares as f64;\n    (base_voting_power as f64 * share_ratio) as u64\n}\n\n// Modify cast_vote method to handle fractional voting\npub async fn cast_vote(\n    &self,\n    proposal_id: Uuid,\n    voter: &str,\n    choice: VoteChoice,\n    signature: &[u8],\n    // NEW: Optional fractional voting parameters\n    fractional_vote: Option<FractionalVoteParams>,\n) -> Result<(), ProposalError> {\n    // ... existing signature verification ...\n\n    let voting_power = match fractional_vote {\n        Some(params) => {\n            // Verify voter owns the shares\n            // Calculate proportional voting power\n            calculate_fractional_voting_power(\n                params.share_token_id,\n                params.shares_to_vote,\n                params.total_supply,\n                params.base_voting_power,\n            )\n        }\n        None => {\n            // Standard voting power calculation\n            1 // or based on token holdings\n        }\n    };\n\n    // ... rest of voting logic with weighted power ...\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct FractionalVoteParams {\n    pub share_token_id: Uuid,\n    pub shares_to_vote: u128,\n    pub total_supply: u128,\n    pub base_voting_power: u64,\n}\n```\n\n### 4.6 Staking Service Changes\n\n**File:** `/app/project/services/staking_service/src/staking_logic.rs`\n\n#### 4.6.1 Fractional Stake Tracking\n\n```rust\n// Modify Staker struct (line 79) to include fractional holdings\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct Staker {\n    pub id: StakerId,\n    pub stake: u128,\n    pub last_active: DateTime<Utc>,\n    pub vrf_pubkey: Vec<u8>,\n    // NEW: Fractional NFT holdings that count toward stake\n    pub fractional_stakes: Vec<FractionalStake>,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct FractionalStake {\n    pub share_token_id: Uuid,\n    pub shares_held: u128,\n    /// Stake value derived from share ownership\n    pub stake_value: u128,\n}\n\nimpl Staker {\n    /// Calculate total effective stake including fractional holdings\n    pub fn effective_stake(&self) -> u128 {\n        let fractional_stake: u128 = self.fractional_stakes\n            .iter()\n            .map(|fs| fs.stake_value)\n            .sum();\n\n        self.stake.saturating_add(fractional_stake)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Core User Flows\n\n### 5.1 Flow A: Owner Fractionalizing Their NFT\n\n#### Sequence of Operations\n\n1. **User initiates fractionalization** via API Gateway\n2. **API Gateway** validates request and forwards to Minting Service\n3. **Minting Service** verifies ownership and creates fractionalization payload\n4. **Minting Service** submits transaction to Node Service\n5. **Node Service** validates and processes the transaction:\n   - Creates vault address for NFT escrow\n   - Generates fractional share token\n   - Mints total shares to owner\n   - Updates NFT state to `Fractionalized`\n6. **Node Service** publishes `FractionalizationCompleted` event\n7. **Event listeners** in Wallet, Marketplace, and Governance services update their state\n\n#### Detailed Flow\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510     \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510 specifying listing and share amount\n3. **API Gateway** forwards to Marketplace Service\n4. **Marketplace Service** validates listing and calculates price\n5. **Marketplace Service** initiates payment verification\n6. **Marketplace Service** submits share transfer to Node Service\n7. **Node Service** processes transfer transaction:\n   - Debits shares from seller\n   - Credits shares to buyer\n   - Handles royalty distribution\n8. **Node Service** publishes `SharesTransferred` event\n9. **Wallet Service** updates both buyer and seller balances\n\n#### Detailed Flow\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510     \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510 section:\n\n```toml\n#######################################################################\n# Fractional NFT Configuration\n#######################################################################\n[fractional]\n# Enable/disable F-NFT feature\nenabled = true\n\n# Minimum shares when fractionalizing (prevents dust)\nmin_shares = 100\n\n# Maximum shares when fractionalizing (prevents overflow)\nmax_shares = 1_000_000_000_000\n\n# Default buyout auction duration in seconds (72 hours)\ndefault_auction_duration_secs = 259200\n\n# Default approval quorum in basis points (50%)\ndefault_approval_quorum_bp = 5000\n\n# Minimum reserve price per share in smallest denomination\nmin_reserve_price = 1\n\n# Fee for fractionalization (basis points)\nfractionalization_fee_bp = 25  # 0.25%\n\n# Fee for reconstitution (basis points)\nreconstitution_fee_bp = 50     # 0.5%\n\n# Share symbol prefix\nsymbol_prefix = \"FNFT-\"\n\n# Maximum symbol length\nmax_symbol_length = 12\n\n# Governance threshold default (basis points of total supply)\ndefault_governance_threshold_bp = 100  # 1%\n\n# Event bus topics\n[fractional.events]\nfractionalized = \"nft.fractionalized\"\nshares_transferred = \"nft.shares.transferred\"\nbuyout_initiated = \"nft.buyout.initiated\"\nbuyout_voted = \"nft.buyout.voted\"\nbuyout_executed = \"nft.buyout.executed\"\nreconstituted = \"nft.reconstituted\"\n\n# Rate limiting\n[fractional.rate_limits]\nfractionalize_per_hour = 10\ntransfer_per_minute = 100\nbuyout_per_day = 5\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Event Bus Integration\n\n### 7.1 New NATS Subjects\n\nFollowing the existing subject hierarchy pattern from ADR-002:\n\n```\nnft.fractional.v1.fractionalized     # NFT was fractionalized\nnft.fractional.v1.shares.transferred # Shares transferred between addresses\nnft.fractional.v1.shares.locked      # Shares locked for governance\nnft.fractional.v1.shares.unlocked    # Shares unlocked after vote\nnft.fractional.v1.buyout.initiated   # Buyout proposal created\nnft.fractional.v1.buyout.voted       # Vote cast on buyout\nnft.fractional.v1.buyout.executed    # Buyout completed\nnft.fractional.v1.reconstituted      # NFT reconstituted from shares\n```\n\n### 7.2 Event Payloads\n\n```rust\n// Add to crate event types\n\n#[derive(Clone, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum FractionalEvent {\n    Fractionalized {\n        nft_id: Uuid,\n        share_token_id: Uuid,\n        owner: WalletAddress,\n        total_shares: u128,\n        vault_address: WalletAddress,\n        tx_hash: String,\n        timestamp: u64,\n    },\n\n    SharesTransferred {\n        share_token_id: Uuid,\n        from: WalletAddress,\n        to: WalletAddress,\n        amount: u128,\n        tx_hash: String,\n        timestamp: u64,\n    },\n\n    BuyoutInitiated {\n        proposal_id: Uuid,\n        share_token_id: Uuid,\n        proposer: WalletAddress,\n        price_per_share: TokenAmount,\n        expires_at: u64,\n        tx_hash: String,\n    },\n\n    BuyoutVoted {\n        proposal_id: Uuid,\n        voter: WalletAddress,\n        approve: bool,\n        voting_shares: u128,\n        tx_hash: String,\n    },\n\n    BuyoutExecuted {\n        proposal_id: Uuid,\n        share_token_id: Uuid,\n        winner: WalletAddress,\n        total_price: TokenAmount,\n        tx_hash: String,\n    },\n\n    Reconstituted {\n        share_token_id: Uuid,\n        nft_id: Uuid,\n        redeemer: WalletAddress,\n        tx_hash: String,\n        timestamp: u64,\n    },\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 8. Security Considerations\n\n### 8.1 Attack Vectors & Mitigations\n\n| Attack Vector | Risk | Mitigation |\n|--------------|------|------------|\n| **Sybil voting** | Attacker creates many addresses to game buyout votes | Require minimum governance threshold; weight votes by shares held |\n| **Flash loan attacks** | Borrow shares, vote, return shares | Implement voting lockup period; snapshot-based voting |\n| **Front-running buyouts** | MEV bots front-run buyout execution | Use commit-reveal scheme for buyout proposals |\n| **Dust share attacks** | Create many tiny listings to spam marketplace | Minimum listing size; listing fees |\n| **Oracle manipulation** | Manipulate price feeds affecting buyout pricing | Use TWAP; multi-oracle aggregation |\n| **Reconstitution griefing** | Collect 99.9% shares, block reconstitution | Forced buyout mechanism with supermajority |\n\n### 8.2 Signature Requirements\n\nAll state-changing operations require:\n1. Valid signature from the transaction initiator\n2. Nonce for replay protection\n3. Timestamp within acceptable drift window\n\n### 8.3 Invariants to Enforce\n\n1. **Share supply invariant**: Sum of all holdings must equal total supply\n2. **Locked share invariant**: Locked shares cannot be transferred\n3. **Vault invariant**: NFT must remain in vault while fractionalized\n4. **Reconstitution invariant**: Only holder of 100% shares can reconstitute\n\n---\n\n## 9. Migration Strategy\n\n### 9.1 Database Migration\n\n1. Create new tables with `IF NOT EXISTS` guards\n2. Add `fractionalization` column to existing `nfts` table as nullable JSON\n3. Backfill existing NFTs with `Whole` state\n4. Create indexes for performance\n\n### 9.2 Service Deployment Order\n\n1. **Phase 1**: Deploy `ccs_common` and `ccs_proto` changes\n2. **Phase 2**: Deploy database migrations\n3. **Phase 3**: Deploy `node_service` with new transaction types (feature-flagged)\n4. **Phase 4**: Deploy `minting_service` with fractionalization logic\n5. **Phase 5**: Deploy `marketplace_service`, `wallet_service` updates\n6. **Phase 6**: Deploy `api_gateway` with new endpoints\n7. **Phase 7**: Enable feature flag; monitor for issues\n8. **Phase 8**: Deploy `governance_service`, `staking_service` updates\n\n### 9.3 Feature Flag\n\nAll F-NFT functionality should be gated by a feature flag:\n\n```rust\n// In each service\nif config.fractional.enabled {\n    // Register F-NFT routes/handlers\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 10. platform. Key points:\n\n1. **Foundation**: Changes start in `ccs_common/src/nft.rs` with new data structures and extend to all services\n2. **State Management**: The `node_service` state machine handles all critical state transitions atomically\n3. **Service Communication**: All inter-service calls follow the existing gRPC + NATS patterns per ADR-002\n4. **Security**: Multiple attack vectors are addressed with signature requirements and voting lockups\n5. **Migration**: Phased deployment with feature flags enables safe rollout\n\nThe implementation team should follow the component-level designs closely, ensuring that:\n- All state changes are validated by the consensus nodes\n- Events are published for all significant state transitions\n- The existing architecture patterns (Factory, Strategy, Observer) are maintained\n- Tests are written for each new transaction type and API endpoint\n",

# Fractional NFT (F-NFT) Integration: Technical Design Document

## CanvasChain Symphony Platform

**Document Version:** 1.0
**Date:** 2026-02-02
**Author:** Lead Architect
**Status:** Draft for Review

---

## Table of Contents

1. [Executive Summary](#1-executive-summary)
2. [Impact Analysis](#2-impact-analysis)
3. [Data Model Changes](#3-data-model-changes)
4. [Component-Level Design](#4-component-level-design)
5. [Core User Flows](#5-core-user-flows)
6. [API & Configuration Changes](#6-api--configuration-changes)
7. [Event Bus Integration](#7-event-bus-integration)
8. [Security Considerations](#8-security-considerations)
9. [Migration Strategy](#9-migration-strategy)
10. [Appendix: Sequence Diagrams](#10-appendix-sequence-diagrams)

---

## 1. Executive Summary

### 1.1 Feature Overview

Fractional NFTs (F-NFTs) enable a single, high-value NFT to be "sharded" into multiple fungible tokens representing partial ownership. This feature aims to:

- **Increase liquidity** for high-value NFTs
- **Democratize access** to expensive digital art
- **Enable collective ownership** and governance of valuable assets

### 1.2 Architectural Approach

The F-NFT feature will be implemented by:

1. **Extending the core NFT data model** in `ccs_common` with fractional ownership metadata
2. **Introducing a new transaction type** (`Transaction::Fractionalize`) in the node service state machine
3. **Creating dedicated gRPC endpoints** in the minting service for fractionalization operations
4. **Modifying the marketplace** to support fractional share listings and trading
5. **Updating the governance service** to handle fractional voting power
6. **Extending the wallet service** to display and manage fractional holdings

---
